### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - 3D Visualization - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 4
**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `dace9c99-2e10-4740-a1f4-681382edf2a6`

**Question:**
> A toy building block is shaped like a cube with edges of 3 cm.

What is the total volume of 4 of these identical blocks?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12 cm³
2. [ ] B) 36 cm³
3. [ ] C) 48 cm³
4. [ ] D) 108 cm³
5. [ ] E) 144 cm³

**Solution:**
> • First, find the volume of one cube: Volume = edge × edge × edge = 3 × 3 × 3 = 27 cm³
• Then multiply by the number of blocks: Total volume = 27 × 4 = 108 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is D because 4 blocks with volume 27 cm³ each have a total volume of 108 cm³

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `48cdc832-f5cc-4fbb-8571-e49a9f04654e`

**Question:**
> A storage company makes moving boxes in the shape of rectangular prisms. A particular box has dimensions 50 cm × 40 cm × 30 cm. The company wants to know how much cardboard is needed to make one box (assuming no overlaps).

What is the total surface area of cardboard needed?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6000 cm²
2. [ ] B) 9400 cm²
3. [ ] C) 11800 cm²
4. [ ] D) 60000 cm²
5. [ ] E) 4700 cm²

**Solution:**
> • Surface area formula: 2(lw + lh + wh) where l=50, w=40, h=30
• Calculate each face area: (50×40) = 2000, (50×30) = 1500, (40×30) = 1200
• Total surface area = 2(2000 + 1500 + 1200) = 2(4700) = 9400 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because 9400 cm² of cardboard is needed to cover all six faces of the box

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c62e5b22-3295-4fa7-b8e8-df392e173157`

**Question:**
> A fish tank is in the shape of a rectangular prism with dimensions 60 cm × 30 cm × 40 cm.

What is the volume of water the tank can hold when completely filled?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 130 cm³
2. [ ] B) 72,000 cm³
3. [ ] C) 7,200 cm³
4. [ ] D) 1,800 cm³
5. [ ] E) 2,400 cm³

**Solution:**
> • Volume of a rectangular prism = length × width × height
• Volume = 60 × 30 × 40
• Volume = 1,800 × 40 = 72,000 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is B because the tank can hold 72,000 cm³ of water when completely filled

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `ece4c3c8-2b11-4a1c-aae0-a52319d759d8`

**Question:**
> A photographer stores camera lenses in protective cube-shaped cases. Each case has an edge length of 10 cm. She needs to wrap each case completely with bubble wrap that costs $0.50 per 100 cm². How much will it cost to wrap one case?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $2.00
2. [ ] B) $3.00
3. [ ] C) $5.00
4. [ ] D) $6.00
5. [ ] E) $10.00

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the surface area of the cube: Surface area = 6 × (edge length)² = 6 × 10² = 6 × 100 = 600 cm²
• Next, calculate the cost: Cost = (600 cm² ÷ 100 cm²) × $0.50 = 6 × $0.50 = $3.00
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total surface area is 600 cm² and at $0.50 per 100 cm², the cost is $3.00

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - Reflections & Transformations - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `65a10753-08ce-4e78-80cc-b1e35d66e4c5`

**Question:**
> A satellite tracking station plots a spacecraft at coordinates (7, -2). Mission control rotates the coordinate system 180° around the origin, then reflects the result across the x-axis. What are the final coordinates of the spacecraft?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (-7, 2)
2. [ ] B) (-7, -2)
3. [ ] C) (7, 2)
4. [ ] D) (7, -2)
5. [ ] E) (-7, 0)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Rotate (7, -2) by 180° around the origin. A 180° rotation changes both coordinates to their opposites: (7, -2) → (-7, 2)
• Step 2: Reflect (-7, 2) across the x-axis. Reflecting across the x-axis keeps the x-coordinate the same and changes the y-coordinate to its opposite: (-7, 2) → (-7, -2)
• Therefore, the answer is B because after both transformations, the spacecraft is at coordinates (-7, -2)

**ID:** `271e6542-436d-4d65-bc35-e4eea339463f`

3. [ ] C) (-4, 6)
4. [ ] D) (-4, -6)
5. [ ] E) (6, -4)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Reflect (4, -6) across the y-axis. This changes the x-coordinate to its opposite while keeping y the same: (4, -6) → (-4, -6)
• Step 2: Rotate (-4, -6) by 180° around the origin. A 180° rotation changes both coordinates to their opposites: (-4, -6) → (4, 6)
• Therefore, the answer is A because after both transformations, the final coordinates are (4, 6)

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - 3D Visualization - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 4
**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `ec602cba-5080-4a23-b95b-b385e18de777`

**Question:**
> A large cube is built from small identical cubes, each with an edge length of 1 cm. The large cube has an edge length of 4 cm. The entire outer surface of the large cube is then painted red.

How many of the small cubes have exactly two faces painted red?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 12
4. [ ] D) 32
5. [ ] E) 16

**Solution:**
> • The large cube is 4 × 4 × 4, containing 64 small cubes total
• Small cubes with exactly 2 painted faces are located along the edges, but not at corners
• Each edge of the large cube has 4 small cubes, but the 2 corner cubes have 3 painted faces
• So each edge has 4 - 2 = 2 small cubes with exactly 2 painted faces
• A cube has 12 edges, so total = 12 × 2 = 24 small cubes
• Therefore, the answer is B because 24 small cubes are positioned along edges with exactly two faces exposed and painted

• Volume = 144 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is C because the volume is found by multiplying all three dimensions together.

How many tennis balls are used in total to build this pyramid?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 20
2. [ ] B) 30
3. [ ] C) 25
4. [ ] D) 16
5. [ ] E) 24

• Second layer: 3×3 = 9 balls
• Third layer: 2×2 = 4 balls
• Top layer: 1×1 = 1 ball
• Total = 16 + 9 + 4 + 1 = 30 balls
• Therefore, the answer is B because we add all the balls in each layer of the square pyramid.

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3f723ab6-cc3b-4754-a178-622edd1845d5`

**Question:**
> A video game convention surveyed 150 attendees about the types of games they play:
• 82 attendees play action games
• 71 attendees play puzzle games
• 38 attendees play both action and puzzle games

How many attendees play neither action nor puzzle games?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 27
2. [ ] B) 35
3. [ ] C) 44
4. [ ] D) 53
5. [ ] E) 115

**Solution:**
> • Attendees who play action OR puzzle games = 82 + 71 - 38 = 115
• Attendees who play neither = Total - (action OR puzzle) = 150 - 115 = 35
• Therefore, the answer is B because 35 attendees play neither type of game

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `020688e5-d646-4c8b-84ac-bb7c180954f3`

**Question:**
> A research station tracked the animals observed by 95 scientists during an Arctic expedition:
• 54 scientists saw seals
• 48 scientists saw whales
• 41 scientists saw polar bears
• 22 scientists saw both seals and whales
• 18 scientists saw both whales and polar bears
• 15 scientists saw both seals and polar bears
• 8 scientists saw all three animals

How many scientists saw none of these three animals?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 8
3. [ ] C) 11
4. [ ] D) 14
5. [ ] E) 17

**Solution:**
> • Using the inclusion-exclusion principle for three sets:
• |Seals ∪ Whales ∪ Polar bears| = 54 + 48 + 41 - 22 - 18 - 15 + 8
• = 143 - 55 + 8 = 96 - 9 = 87 scientists saw at least one animal
• Scientists who saw none = Total scientists - Scientists who saw at least one
• = 95 - 87 = 8 scientists
• Therefore, the answer is B because 8 scientists saw none of these three animals

5. [ ] E) 65

• Those who bought both fiction and non-fiction = 15

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - Reflections & Transformations - multiple_choice

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0f8079e0-ce6d-4715-ba79-a3fb4423124c`

**Question:**
> A park ranger marks a campsite at coordinates C(−2, 5) on a park map. The campsite location is reflected across the y-axis to find a matching site on the opposite side of the valley. What are the new coordinates of the reflected campsite?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (2, 5)
2. [ ] B) (−2, −5)
3. [ ] C) (2, −5)
4. [ ] D) (−5, 2)
5. [ ] E) (5, −2)

**Solution:**
> • When reflecting across the y-axis, the y-coordinate stays the same and the x-coordinate changes to its opposite
• The original campsite is at C(−2, 5)
• Reflecting across the y-axis: x-coordinate changes from −2 to 2, y-coordinate remains 5
• Therefore, the answer is A because the reflected campsite is at (2, 5)

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `f5dd6865-7bea-404b-aff8-35b4ed9804a5`

**Question:**
> A telescope observes a star at position S(−2, 6) on an astronomical grid. The star's position is first reflected across the x-axis, then reflected across the line y = x. What are the final coordinates of the star?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (−6, 2)
2. [ ] B) (−6, −2)
3. [ ] C) (6, 2)
4. [ ] D) (2, −6)
5. [ ] E) (−2, −6)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Reflect S(−2, 6) across the x-axis. This keeps the x-coordinate the same and changes the sign of the y-coordinate: (−2, 6) → (−2, −6)
• Step 2: Reflect (−2, −6) across the line y = x. This transformation swaps the x and y coordinates: (−2, −6) → (−6, −2)
• Therefore, the answer is B because after both transformations, the star's final position is (−6, −2)

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `40d22b34-6b63-4a93-be56-45519fff77f9`

2. [ ] B) (−3, −4)
3. [ ] C) (3, −4)
4. [ ] D) (−3, 4)
5. [ ] E) (4, −3)

**Solution:**
> • When reflecting across the y-axis, the y-coordinate stays the same and the x-coordinate changes to its opposite
• The original position is C(−3, 4)
• Reflecting across the y-axis: x-coordinate changes from −3 to 3, y-coordinate stays 4
• Therefore, the answer is A because the new coordinates are (3, 4)

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `6f3b9ee1-0acd-4024-8833-07fb488fe49c`

**Question:**
> A robot on a factory floor is at position R(−5, 2). The robot is first reflected across the y-axis, then rotated 180° around the origin. What are the final coordinates of the robot?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (5, 2)
2. [ ] B) (−5, −2)
3. [ ] C) (5, −2)
4. [ ] D) (−5, 2)
5. [ ] E) (−2, 5)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Reflect R(−5, 2) across the y-axis. This changes the x-coordinate to its opposite while keeping the y-coordinate the same: (5, 2).
• Step 2: Rotate (5, 2) by 180° around the origin. A 180° rotation changes both coordinates to their opposites: (−5, −2).
• Therefore, the answer is B because after reflecting across the y-axis and then rotating 180°, the final position is (−5, −2).

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `eb913b7a-f062-4209-8cb2-59cdf9fbdbd9`

**Question:**
> A marine biologist tracks a dolphin at position D(−4, 6) on an ocean grid. The dolphin's position is first reflected across the x-axis, then reflected across the y-axis, and finally the result is rotated 180° around the origin. What are the final coordinates of the dolphin?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (4, −6)
2. [ ] B) (−4, 6)
3. [ ] C) (4, 6)
4. [ ] D) (−4, −6)
5. [ ] E) (6, −4)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Reflect D(−4, 6) across the x-axis: the x-coordinate stays the same, y-coordinate changes sign → (−4, −6)
• Step 2: Reflect (−4, −6) across the y-axis: the y-coordinate stays the same, x-coordinate changes sign → (4, −6)
• Step 3: Rotate (4, −6) by 180° around the origin: both coordinates change sign → (−4, 6)
• Therefore, the answer is B because after all three transformations, the dolphin returns to its original position (−4, 6)

**ID:** `82447bb2-fb01-4186-aa14-1c90c5091966`

**Question:**
> A camping store surveyed 135 customers about the outdoor equipment they own:
• 76 customers own a tent
• 62 customers own a sleeping bag
• 29 customers own both a tent and a sleeping bag

How many customers own neither a tent nor a sleeping bag?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 21
2. [ ] B) 26
3. [ ] C) 33
4. [ ] D) 47
5. [ ] E) 109

**Solution:**
> • Customers who own a tent OR a sleeping bag = 76 + 62 - 29 = 109
• Customers who own neither = Total - (tent OR sleeping bag) = 135 - 109 = 26
• Therefore, the answer is B because 26 customers own neither item

5. [ ] E) 96

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `726e0615-0125-451f-982a-5a6f908faed3`

**Question:**
> A research team studied 105 ancient artifacts discovered at an archaeological site:
• 58 artifacts were made of pottery
• 49 artifacts were decorated with patterns
• 44 artifacts were tools
• 22 artifacts were pottery with patterns
• 18 artifacts were pottery tools
• 15 artifacts were decorated tools
• 8 artifacts were pottery tools with patterns

How many artifacts were none of these three types (not pottery, not decorated, and not tools)?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 9
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 15
4. [ ] D) 18
5. [ ] E) 21

**Solution:**
> • Using the inclusion-exclusion principle for three sets:
• |Pottery ∪ Decorated ∪ Tools| = 58 + 49 + 44 - 22 - 18 - 15 + 8
• = 151 - 55 + 8 = 104 - 11 = 93 artifacts that are at least one type
• Artifacts that are none of these = Total - (at least one type) = 105 - 93 = 12
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 artifacts were none of the three types

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - 3D Visualization - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 4
**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `76553691-9f4e-4fb2-a156-8a3ae67f6ff9`

**Question:**
> A large cube made of 27 smaller identical cubes is dipped into purple paint so that all exposed surfaces are painted. After the paint dries, the large cube is separated back into the 27 smaller cubes.

How many of the small cubes have exactly 2 faces painted?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 1
5. [ ] E) 0

**Solution:**
> • A large cube made of 27 small cubes has dimensions 3×3×3
• Small cubes with exactly 2 painted faces are located on the edges but NOT at corners
• Each edge of the large cube has 3 small cubes: 2 corners (with 3 painted faces) and 1 middle cube (with 2 painted faces)
• A cube has 12 edges, so there are 12 edge-middle cubes with exactly 2 painted faces
• Therefore, the answer is B because there are 12 small cubes with exactly 2 faces painted

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `fd79a5d7-bf7c-4b53-966b-5fed389d15a4`

**Question:**
> A museum displays ancient stone blocks. Each block is a rectangular prism with dimensions 8 cm × 5 cm × 4 cm. What is the total surface area of one block?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 160 cm²
2. [ ] B) 184 cm²
3. [ ] C) 192 cm²
4. [ ] D) 200 cm²
5. [ ] E) 208 cm²

**Solution:**
> • Surface area of a rectangular prism = 2(lw + lh + wh)
• Calculate each face area: (8×5) = 40, (8×4) = 32, (5×4) = 20
• Sum of face areas: 40 + 32 + 20 = 92
• Total surface area: 2 × 92 = 184 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because the block has 6 faces (2 of each dimension pair) with total area 184 cm²

---

**ID:** `6415c25e-d123-4c1f-9041-1a3e24e696b3`

What is the volume of the brick?

1. [ ] A) 35 cm³
2. [ ] B) 100 cm³
3. [ ] C) 200 cm³
4. [ ] D) 1000 cm³
5. [ ] E) 1500 cm³

**Solution:**
> • Volume of a rectangular prism = length × width × height
• Volume = 20 × 10 × 5 = 1000 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is D because the volume of the brick is 1000 cm³

What is the total volume of all three shelves combined?

2. [ ] B) 120,000 cm³
3. [ ] C) 125,000 cm³
4. [ ] D) 160,000 cm³
5. [ ] E) 240,000 cm³

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the volume of one shelf: 80 × 25 × 20 = 40,000 cm³
• Since there are 3 identical shelves, multiply by 3: 40,000 × 3 = 120,000 cm³

To create a symmetrical exhibition, the sculpture's position is first reflected across the x-axis, then the resulting position is reflected across the line y = x (which swaps the x and y coordinates). What are the final coordinates of the sculpture's position?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (−2, 4)
2. [ ] B) (−2, −4)
3. [ ] C) (2, −4)
4. [ ] D) (4, −2)
5. [ ] E) (−4, −2)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Reflect S(−4, 2) across the x-axis. This keeps the x-coordinate the same and changes the y-coordinate to its opposite: (−4, −2)
• Step 2: Reflect (−4, −2) across the line y = x. This transformation swaps the x and y coordinates: (−2, −4)
• Therefore, the answer is B because after both transformations, the sculpture's final position is (−2, −4)

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d2808527-17ed-4348-b928-64767df87e69`

**Question:**
> A large cube is made from 64 smaller identical cubes arranged in a 4×4×4 formation. The large cube is then painted blue on all its outer faces. How many of the small cubes will have exactly 1 face painted blue?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 32
4. [ ] D) 48
5. [ ] E) 56

**Solution:**
> • Small cubes with exactly 1 painted face are located in the center of each face of the large cube (not on edges or corners)
• Each face of the 4×4×4 cube shows a 4×4 grid of small cubes
• On each face, the cubes with only 1 painted face form a 2×2 square in the middle (excluding the outer ring which touches edges)
• So each face contributes 2×2 = 4 small cubes with exactly 1 painted face
• A cube has 6 faces, so total = 6 × 4 = 24 small cubes
• Therefore, the answer is B because 24 small cubes have exactly 1 face painted blue

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `1e06f6f4-7696-46a2-9c7b-c643eb70ff88`

**Question:**
> A construction company builds a concrete pillar in the shape of a rectangular prism with dimensions 2 m × 2 m × 5 m. The pillar needs to be painted on all its exterior surfaces except the bottom, which will be embedded in the ground.

What is the total surface area that needs to be painted?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 20 m²
2. [ ] B) 36 m²
3. [ ] C) 44 m²
4. [ ] D) 48 m²
5. [ ] E) 52 m²

**Solution:**
> • The pillar is a rectangular prism with dimensions 2 m × 2 m × 5 m
• Total surface area = 2(lw + lh + wh) = 2(2×2 + 2×5 + 2×5) = 2(4 + 10 + 10) = 2(24) = 48 m²
• The bottom face (which won't be painted) has area = 2 × 2 = 4 m²
• Surface area to be painted = 48 - 4 = 44 m²
• Therefore, the answer is C because 44 m² of surface area needs to be painted

> A refrigerator has three compartments. The main compartment measures 60 cm × 50 cm × 80 cm, the middle compartment measures 60 cm × 50 cm × 30 cm, and the freezer measures 60 cm × 50 cm × 40 cm.

What is the total volume of all three compartments combined?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 190 cm³
2. [ ] B) 450,000 cm³
3. [ ] C) 240,000 cm³
4. [ ] D) 150,000 cm³
5. [ ] E) 360,000 cm³

**Solution:**
> • Volume of main compartment = 60 × 50 × 80 = 240,000 cm³
• Volume of middle compartment = 60 × 50 × 30 = 90,000 cm³
• Volume of freezer = 60 × 50 × 40 = 120,000 cm³
• Total volume = 240,000 + 90,000 + 120,000 = 450,000 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is B because the combined volume of all three compartments is 450,000 cm³

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3e7a9d24-b452-4354-ac42-6841fc089f50`

**Question:**
> A botanical garden recorded the trees in their collection:
• 35 trees produce fruit
• 28 trees have colorful flowers
• 14 trees both produce fruit and have colorful flowers
• 8 trees neither produce fruit nor have colorful flowers

How many trees are in the collection?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 57
2. [ ] B) 63
3. [ ] C) 71
4. [ ] D) 85
5. [ ] E) 49

**Solution:**
> • Trees that only produce fruit = 35 - 14 = 21
• Trees that only have colorful flowers = 28 - 14 = 14
• Trees that have both features = 14
• Trees with neither feature = 8
• Total trees = 21 + 14 + 14 + 8 = 57
• Therefore, the answer is A because we must count each group separately: only fruit (21), only flowers (14), both (14), and neither (8), which gives us 57 trees in total.

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/diagnostic - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - Reflections & Transformations - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `df747ba2-d0ee-41ea-bb4d-88fe5ab077f8`

**Question:**
> A wildlife researcher tracks a bird's nest at position N(−7, 2) on a forest grid. The position is reflected across the y-axis to mark a symmetrical observation point. What are the coordinates of the new observation point?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (7, −2)
2. [ ] B) (7, 2)
3. [ ] C) (−7, −2)
4. [ ] D) (−7, 2)
5. [ ] E) (2, −7)

**Solution:**
> • When reflecting across the y-axis, the y-coordinate stays the same and the x-coordinate changes to its opposite
• The original position is N(−7, 2)
• Reflecting across the y-axis: x-coordinate changes from −7 to 7, y-coordinate stays 2
• Therefore, the answer is B because the new coordinates are (7, 2)

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c8ab28d9-5917-4c55-879e-dff025532fca`

**Question:**
> A pilot marks a checkpoint at position C(4, −6) on a flight grid. The checkpoint is first rotated 180° around the origin, then the result is reflected across the x-axis.

What are the final coordinates of the checkpoint?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (−4, −6)
2. [ ] B) (−4, 6)
3. [ ] C) (4, 6)
4. [ ] D) (4, −6)
5. [ ] E) (−6, 4)

**Solution:**
> • Step 1: Rotate C(4, −6) by 180° around the origin. A 180° rotation changes (x, y) to (−x, −y), so (4, −6) becomes (−4, 6).
• Step 2: Reflect (−4, 6) across the x-axis. Reflection across the x-axis keeps the x-coordinate the same and negates the y-coordinate, so (−4, 6) becomes (−4, −6).
• Therefore, the answer is A because after both transformations, the checkpoint is at (−4, −6).

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `fd0877d7-23f3-4a2f-96de-ba0c6b696e02`

**Question:**
> A hot air balloon is floating at position B(2, 9) on a festival tracking grid.

If the balloon's position is reflected across the x-axis, what are the new coordinates?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (-2, 9)
2. [ ] B) (2, -9)
3. [ ] C) (-2, -9)
4. [ ] D) (9, 2)
5. [ ] E) (2, 9)

**Solution:**
> • When reflecting across the x-axis, the x-coordinate stays the same while the y-coordinate changes to its opposite
• The original position is (2, 9)
• The x-coordinate remains 2, and the y-coordinate becomes -9
• Therefore, the answer is B because (2, 9) reflected across the x-axis becomes (2, -9)

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `32ad90ba-a470-4059-84d3-37bc74001026`

**Question:**
> A skateboarder marks a trick location at position T(-5, -3) on a skate park grid. The location is reflected across the x-axis. What are the new coordinates of the trick location?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) (5, -3)
2. [ ] B) (-5, 3)
3. [ ] C) (5, 3)
4. [ ] D) (-5, -3)
5. [ ] E) (3, -5)

**Solution:**
> • When reflecting across the x-axis, the x-coordinate stays the same and the y-coordinate changes to its opposite
• Original position: T(-5, -3)
• After reflection across x-axis: x-coordinate remains -5, y-coordinate becomes -(-3) = 3
• Therefore, the answer is B because the new coordinates are (-5, 3)

### ACER Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/diagnostic - Mathematics - Spatial Reasoning - 3D Visualization - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 4
**Sampled Questions:** 4

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b3b0476e-eb2e-4f56-9db7-e4bf89cae24b`

**Question:**
> A sports equipment store stacks tennis ball cans on a shelf. Each can is shaped like a cylinder, but for storage purposes, the store treats them as rectangular prisms with dimensions 7 cm × 7 cm × 20 cm.

If the shelf space available is 28 cm × 21 cm × 20 cm, how many cans can fit on this shelf?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 16
4. [ ] D) 20
5. [ ] E) 24

**Solution:**
> • First, find how many cans fit along the length: 28 ÷ 7 = 4 cans
• Next, find how many cans fit along the width: 21 ÷ 7 = 3 cans
• Finally, find how many cans fit along the height: 20 ÷ 20 = 1 layer
• Total number of cans = 4 × 3 × 1 = 12 cans
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 cans can fit on the shelf

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `5356861d-3634-48ca-84c7-8c84576b61a1`

**Question:**
> A glass aquarium is shaped like a rectangular prism with dimensions 50 cm × 30 cm × 40 cm. The aquarium is filled with water to 60% of its capacity. A decorative rock with a volume of 6000 cm³ is then placed into the aquarium, causing the water level to rise.

What is the new percentage of the aquarium's capacity that is filled with water after the rock is added?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 66%
2. [ ] B) 70%
3. [ ] C) 72%
4. [ ] D) 75%
5. [ ] E) 78%

**Solution:**
> • Total volume of aquarium = 50 × 30 × 40 = 60,000 cm³
• Initial water volume = 60% of 60,000 = 0.60 × 60,000 = 36,000 cm³
• Volume of rock = 6,000 cm³
• When the rock is submerged, it displaces water, raising the level. The combined volume of water and rock = 36,000 + 6,000 = 42,000 cm³
• New percentage filled = (42,000 ÷ 60,000) × 100% = 0.70 × 100% = 70%
• Therefore, the answer is B because the water and rock together occupy 70% of the aquarium's total capacity

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `69c4b477-81e3-49c6-9d3b-a27d2c06301f`

**Question:**
> A company manufactures candles in the shape of rectangular prisms. Each candle has dimensions 8 cm × 5 cm × 12 cm. The company needs to wrap each candle completely in decorative foil.

What is the minimum area of foil needed to wrap one candle?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 480 cm²
2. [ ] B) 392 cm²
3. [ ] C) 196 cm²
4. [ ] D) 272 cm²
5. [ ] E) 240 cm²

**Solution:**
> • To wrap the candle completely, we need to find the total surface area of the rectangular prism
• Surface area formula: 2(lw + lh + wh) where l=8, w=5, h=12
• Calculate each face pair: Top/Bottom = 2(8×5) = 80 cm², Front/Back = 2(8×12) = 192 cm², Left/Right = 2(5×12) = 120 cm²
• Total surface area = 80 + 192 + 120 = 392 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because 392 cm² of foil is needed to completely wrap one candle

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d302209c-8e56-4d37-aeb8-984199717d11`

**Question:**
> A cube-shaped gift box has edges of 4 cm. What is the volume of the gift box?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12 cm³
2. [ ] B) 16 cm³
3. [ ] C) 48 cm³
4. [ ] D) 64 cm³
5. [ ] E) 96 cm³

**Solution:**
> • Volume of a cube = edge × edge × edge
• Volume = 4 × 4 × 4 = 64 cm³
• Therefore, the answer is D because the volume of a cube with 4 cm edges is 64 cm³

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Applied Word Problems - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0aa09956-1f80-49ef-9342-56be886f4576`

**Question:**
> A school fundraiser sells raffle tickets at $3 each. They sold 85 tickets on Friday and 127 tickets on Saturday. If the prize costs $150 and the rest is donated to charity, how much money is donated?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $486
2. [ ] B) $486
3. [ ] C) $636
4. [ ] D) $381
5. [ ] E) $212

**Solution:**
> • Total tickets sold: 85 + 127 = 212 tickets
• Total money raised: 212 × $3 = $636
• Money donated to charity: $636 - $150 = $486
• Therefore, the answer is A because after subtracting the prize cost from total revenue, $486 is donated to charity

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3fc022da-e3fe-407d-a543-c694d59c076a`

**Question:**
> A basketball game starts at 2:15 PM and lasts for 1 hour and 40 minutes. If the players need to arrive 30 minutes before the game starts, what time should they arrive?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 1:45 PM
2. [ ] B) 1:30 PM
3. [ ] C) 2:45 PM
4. [ ] D) 3:55 PM
5. [ ] E) 3:25 PM

**Solution:**
> • Game starts at 2:15 PM
• Players need to arrive 30 minutes before: 2:15 PM - 30 minutes = 1:45 PM
• Therefore, the answer is A because the players should arrive at 1:45 PM

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `04bb8d70-ac60-4bd2-ac67-44c5c1e4e0aa`

**Question:**
> A zoo keeper feeds the penguins 3 buckets of fish in the morning and 5 buckets in the afternoon. Each bucket contains 24 fish. How many fish do the penguins eat in one day?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 72
2. [ ] B) 192
3. [ ] C) 120
4. [ ] D) 168
5. [ ] E) 96

**Solution:**
> • Total buckets per day = 3 + 5 = 8 buckets
• Total fish = 8 × 24 = 192 fish
• Therefore, the answer is B because the penguins eat 192 fish in one day

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `96d30d1e-6a06-40a9-a8c3-9a7e178ac95b`

**Question:**
> A juice box contains 250 millilitres. A school orders 8 packs of juice boxes, with each pack containing 6 juice boxes. How many litres of juice did the school order in total?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2 litres
2. [ ] B) 12 litres
3. [ ] C) 48 litres
4. [ ] D) 1.5 litres
5. [ ] E) 120 litres

**Solution:**
> • Total number of juice boxes = 8 packs × 6 boxes per pack = 48 juice boxes
• Total volume in millilitres = 48 boxes × 250 mL = 12,000 mL
• Convert to litres: 12,000 mL ÷ 1,000 = 12 litres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the school ordered 12 litres of juice in total

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e0bb5578-5fea-4063-af35-e3811be646d6`

**Question:**
> A bookstore offers a 15% discount on all books during a sale. Marcus buys 4 books that originally cost $18 each. He pays with a $100 note. How much change should he receive?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $28.60
2. [ ] B) $38.80
3. [ ] C) $61.20
4. [ ] D) $72.00
5. [ ] E) $10.80

**Solution:**
> • Original total cost: 4 × $18 = $72
• Discount amount: 15% of $72 = 0.15 × $72 = $10.80
• Sale price: $72 - $10.80 = $61.20
• Change from $100: $100 - $61.20 = $38.80
• Therefore, the answer is B because Marcus receives $38.80 in change

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Fractions & Mixed Numbers - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d1531056-a3ba-45bd-bd9e-e2e96af226ad`

**Question:**
> A builder needs to cut a wooden plank that is 8 1/3 metres long into pieces that are each 1 2/5 metres long. How many complete pieces can be cut from the plank?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 7
4. [ ] D) 5 pieces with 6/7 metre remaining
5. [ ] E) 6 pieces with 1/15 metre remaining

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 8 1/3 = 25/3 and 1 2/5 = 7/5
• Divide to find how many pieces: 25/3 ÷ 7/5 = 25/3 × 5/7 = 125/21
• Convert 125/21 to a mixed number: 125 ÷ 21 = 5 remainder 20, so 5 20/21
• Since we need complete pieces only, the answer is 5 complete pieces
• Therefore, the answer is A because only 5 complete pieces of 1 2/5 metres can be cut from the 8 1/3 metre plank

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `72eae536-d76f-4386-9e28-42ee9afc40fa`

**Question:**
> Convert the improper fraction 47/8 to a mixed number.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5 7/8
2. [ ] B) 5 5/8
3. [ ] C) 6 7/8
4. [ ] D) 4 7/8
5. [ ] E) 5 3/4

**Solution:**
> • Divide 47 by 8: 47 ÷ 8 = 5 remainder 7
• The whole number is 5, and the remainder becomes the numerator: 7
• The denominator stays the same: 8
• Therefore, the answer is A because 47/8 = 5 7/8

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `f4e96b9e-2f69-4d07-b5e0-3ca96c6956cd`

**Question:**
> Divide: 5 1/4 ÷ 3/8 =

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12
2. [ ] B) 14
3. [ ] C) 1 31/32
4. [ ] D) 15 3/4
5. [ ] E) 2 1/8

**Solution:**
> • Convert 5 1/4 to an improper fraction: 5 1/4 = 21/4
• Dividing by a fraction means multiplying by its reciprocal: 21/4 ÷ 3/8 = 21/4 × 8/3
• Multiply: (21 × 8)/(4 × 3) = 168/12
• Simplify: 168/12 = 14
• Therefore, the answer is B because 5 1/4 ÷ 3/8 = 14

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `ae919a96-606d-4a1d-9bb7-bb11d7c07cf3`

**Question:**
> Calculate: 4 1/6 - 1 3/4 =

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2 5/12
2. [ ] B) 2 5/6
3. [ ] C) 3 5/12
4. [ ] D) 2 7/12
5. [ ] E) 3 7/12

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 4 1/6 = 25/6 and 1 3/4 = 7/4
• Find common denominator (LCD of 6 and 4 is 12): 25/6 = 50/12 and 7/4 = 21/12
• Subtract: 50/12 - 21/12 = 29/12
• Convert to mixed number: 29/12 = 2 5/12
• Therefore, the answer is A because 4 1/6 - 1 3/4 = 2 5/12

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e635037f-1aab-4cd8-a702-dedef7de3dac`

**Question:**
> Subtract the fractions: 5/6 - 1/3 =

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4/3
2. [ ] B) 1/2
3. [ ] C) 4/6
4. [ ] D) 2/3
5. [ ] E) 1/6

**Solution:**
> • First, find a common denominator. The LCD of 6 and 3 is 6.
• Convert 1/3 to sixths: 1/3 = 2/6
• Subtract: 5/6 - 2/6 = 3/6
• Simplify: 3/6 = 1/2
• Therefore, the answer is B because 5/6 - 1/3 = 1/2

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Fractions & Mixed Numbers - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `bccc34d0-c0fd-4816-a2fb-4520b608f58f`

**Question:**
> A photographer printed 3/5 of her photos in colour and 1/4 of her photos in black and white. What fraction of her photos did she print in total?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4/9
2. [ ] B) 17/20
3. [ ] C) 4/20
4. [ ] D) 17/10
5. [ ] E) 8/9

**Solution:**
> • Find a common denominator for 3/5 and 1/4. The LCD of 5 and 4 is 20
• Convert both fractions: 3/5 = 12/20 and 1/4 = 5/20
• Add the fractions: 12/20 + 5/20 = 17/20
• Therefore, the answer is B because the photographer printed 17/20 of her photos in total

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b67b69a8-9b0b-4b5a-a64b-3dbc2aed3218`

**Question:**
> A marine biologist studied two whales. The first whale weighed 5 3/8 tonnes and the second whale weighed 3 1/4 tonnes. How much heavier was the first whale than the second?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2 1/8 tonnes
2. [ ] B) 2 1/4 tonnes
3. [ ] C) 2 5/8 tonnes
4. [ ] D) 8 5/8 tonnes
5. [ ] E) 2 2/12 tonnes

**Solution:**
> • Convert both mixed numbers to improper fractions or work with common denominators
• Find common denominator: 5 3/8 - 3 1/4 = 5 3/8 - 3 2/8 (converting 1/4 to 2/8)
• Subtract whole numbers: 5 - 3 = 2
• Subtract fractions: 3/8 - 2/8 = 1/8
• Therefore, the answer is A because 2 + 1/8 = 2 1/8 tonnes

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `694cd05d-3ae7-4b76-8bb4-ac08f1a9627b`

**Question:**
> A weather station recorded 2 1/8 centimetres of rainfall on Monday and 1 3/4 centimetres of rainfall on Tuesday. How much more rainfall was recorded on Monday than on Tuesday?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3/8 cm
2. [ ] B) 5/8 cm
3. [ ] C) 1/2 cm
4. [ ] D) 7/8 cm
5. [ ] E) 1 3/8 cm

**Solution:**
> • Convert both mixed numbers to improper fractions or find the difference using common denominators.
• 2 1/8 = 17/8 and 1 3/4 = 7/4 = 14/8 (converting to eighths)
• Subtract: 17/8 - 14/8 = 3/8
• Therefore, the answer is A because Monday had 3/8 cm more rainfall than Tuesday.

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `519ea4c2-7ff5-4e79-951a-f19029cba48b`

**Question:**
> A fabric designer needs 5 1/3 metres of silk to make one scarf. How many complete scarves can be made from 18 2/5 metres of silk?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3
2. [ ] B) 4
3. [ ] C) 3 1/2
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 2

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 5 1/3 = 16/3 and 18 2/5 = 92/5
• Divide: 92/5 ÷ 16/3 = 92/5 × 3/16 = 276/80 = 69/20
• Convert to mixed number: 69/20 = 3 9/20
• Since only complete scarves can be made, the answer is 3
• Therefore, the answer is A because 3 complete scarves can be made (with 9/20 of the fabric needed for a fourth scarf remaining)

3. [ ] C) 5 4/6
4. [ ] D) 4 3/6
5. [ ] E) 3 5/6

• The whole number is 4, the remainder 5 becomes the numerator, and the denominator stays as 6

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Decimals & Decimal Operations - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `30dba207-5c83-40fc-acc5-00d16e820fa7`

**Question:**
> A racing car travels 456.8 kilometres in a time trial. The distance is divided by 100 to convert it into hectometres. What is the distance in hectometres?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4.568
2. [ ] B) 45.68
3. [ ] C) 4568
4. [ ] D) 0.4568
5. [ ] E) 456.8

**Solution:**
> • Dividing by 100 moves the decimal point 2 places to the left
• 456.8 ÷ 100 = 4.568
• Therefore, the answer is A because moving the decimal point 2 places left in 456.8 gives 4.568 hectometres

**ID:** `67bf1535-060a-4c28-b894-b398a21704c1`

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 26.5
2. [ ] B) 2650
3. [ ] C) 265
4. [ ] D) 26500
5. [ ] E) 0.265

**Solution:**

• 2.65 × 1000 = 2650
• Therefore, the answer is B because the baker uses 2650 grams of flour

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `7cd13e6c-3c72-496a-8466-8e7275140c7b`

**Question:**
> A scientist measures the mass of a rare butterfly as 3.45 grams. She needs to record this measurement in kilograms for her research paper. What is 3.45 ÷ 1000?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 0.00345
2. [ ] B) 0.0345
3. [ ] C) 0.345
4. [ ] D) 34.5
5. [ ] E) 0.000345

**Solution:**
> • When dividing by 1000, move the decimal point 3 places to the left
• Starting with 3.45, move the decimal point: 3.45 → 0.345 → 0.0345 → 0.00345
• Therefore, the answer is A because 3.45 ÷ 1000 = 0.00345 kilograms

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `85dd3d77-e93e-4fa7-a210-f72db00eec30`

**Question:**
> A carpenter measures three wooden planks with lengths 4.75 metres, 3.8 metres, and 6.25 metres. What is the total length of all three planks?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 14.8 metres
2. [ ] B) 14.7 metres
3. [ ] C) 15.8 metres
4. [ ] D) 13.8 metres
5. [ ] E) 14.0 metres

**Solution:**
> • Align the decimal points and add: 4.75 + 3.8 + 6.25
• Convert to same decimal places: 4.75 + 3.80 + 6.25
• Add: 4.75 + 3.80 = 8.55, then 8.55 + 6.25 = 14.80 = 14.8
• Therefore, the answer is A because the total length is 14.8 metres

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2b7c7c59-3f10-4ad8-b5cf-b96ae94317f4`

**Question:**
> A jeweller cuts a silver wire that is 8.4 metres long into pieces that are each 0.12 metres long. How many pieces can be cut from the wire?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7
2. [ ] B) 70
3. [ ] C) 700
4. [ ] D) 0.7
5. [ ] E) 84

**Solution:**
> • Divide the total length by the length of each piece: 8.4 ÷ 0.12
• Convert to whole numbers by multiplying both by 100: 840 ÷ 12 = 70
• Alternatively: 8.4 ÷ 0.12 = 8.4 × (100/12) = 840/12 = 70
• Therefore, the answer is B because 70 pieces can be cut from the wire

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Algebra & Equation Solving - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d543fe8b-2c8e-43c8-9119-84fc06337f55`

**Question:**
> A robotics team is building a machine. The total cost in dollars is calculated using the formula 5(n + 3) - 8, where n is the number of parts used. If the total cost was $67, how many parts were used?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 10
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 15
4. [ ] D) 8
5. [ ] E) 18

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: 5(n + 3) - 8 = 67
• Add 8 to both sides: 5(n + 3) = 75
• Divide both sides by 5: n + 3 = 15
• Subtract 3 from both sides: n = 12
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 parts were used

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `8f234d50-4dd1-4d86-8083-0ecef9b3ba61`

**Question:**
> A mountain climber descends from a peak at a steady rate. After 3 hours, her altitude is given by the expression 2400 - 150h meters, where h is the number of hours since she started. If her altitude is now 1200 meters, how many hours has she been descending?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 8
3. [ ] C) 6
4. [ ] D) 12
5. [ ] E) 10

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: 2400 - 150h = 1200
• Subtract 2400 from both sides: -150h = 1200 - 2400 = -1200
• Divide both sides by -150: h = -1200 ÷ -150 = 8
• Therefore, the answer is B because she has been descending for 8 hours

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2d3c32b6-10e4-4918-ad13-6acc08d611ee`

**Question:**
> A video game awards p points for each level completed. Find the value of: 3p - 5 when p = 7

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 11
2. [ ] B) 16
3. [ ] C) 26
4. [ ] D) 19
5. [ ] E) 14

**Solution:**
> • Substitute p = 7 into the expression: 3p - 5
• Calculate: 3(7) - 5 = 21 - 5 = 16
• Therefore, the answer is B because when p = 7, the expression 3p - 5 equals 16

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `291b9639-a057-4b86-b2c9-413c8baf3607`

**Question:**
> A garden designer plants flowers in rows. Each row contains the same number of flowers. If 4 rows plus 7 extra flowers gives a total of 43 flowers, how many flowers are in each row?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7
2. [ ] B) 9
3. [ ] C) 10
4. [ ] D) 12
5. [ ] E) 8

**Solution:**
> • Let x = number of flowers in each row
• Set up equation: 4x + 7 = 43
• Subtract 7 from both sides: 4x = 36
• Divide both sides by 4: x = 9
• Therefore, the answer is B because there are 9 flowers in each row

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c39e38f0-be0e-4a59-9179-b54c38a9f9db`

**Question:**
> A library charges a membership fee of $8 plus $2 for each book borrowed. If Maya paid $24 in total, how many books did she borrow? Solve for b in the equation: 8 + 2b = 24

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 8
3. [ ] C) 10
4. [ ] D) 12
5. [ ] E) 16

**Solution:**
> • Start with the equation: 8 + 2b = 24
• Subtract 8 from both sides: 2b = 24 - 8 = 16
• Divide both sides by 2: b = 16 ÷ 2 = 8
• Therefore, the answer is B because Maya borrowed 8 books

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/diagnostic - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `71bb55fa-d327-481d-9aec-2a4996c37751`

**Question:**
> A triangular park has angles measuring 65° and 48°. What is the measure of the third angle?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 57°
2. [ ] B) 67°
3. [ ] C) 77°
4. [ ] D) 87°
5. [ ] E) 97°

**Solution:**
> • The sum of all angles in any triangle is 180°
• The two known angles are 65° and 48°
• Third angle = 180° - 65° - 48° = 180° - 113° = 67°
• Therefore, the answer is B because the third angle must be 67° to make the total 180°

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9133f43d-aa03-4ad3-9699-203e486b960a`

**Question:**
> A square playground has a perimeter of 48 metres. What is the length of one side of the playground?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8 metres
2. [ ] B) 12 metres
3. [ ] C) 16 metres
4. [ ] D) 24 metres
5. [ ] E) 192 metres

**Solution:**
> • A square has 4 equal sides
• Perimeter = 4 × side length
• 48 = 4 × side length
• Side length = 48 ÷ 4 = 12 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because each side of the square playground measures 12 metres

---

2. [ ] B) 144 m²
3. [ ] C) 72 m²
4. [ ] D) 26 m²
5. [ ] E) 288 m²

**Solution:**
> • The area of a parallelogram is calculated using the formula: Area = base × height
• Given: base = 18 metres, height = 8 metres
• Area = 18 × 8 = 144 square metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of the parallelogram-shaped billboard is 144 m²

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 28 metres
2. [ ] B) 7 metres
3. [ ] C) 14 metres
4. [ ] D) 21 metres
5. [ ] E) 3.5 metres

**Solution:**
> • The radius of a circle is half the diameter
• Radius = Diameter ÷ 2
• Radius = 14 ÷ 2 = 7 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the radius is half of the diameter

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `30040119-1e55-4e55-8e0b-8fd7ee6ee06f`

**Question:**
> A regular hexagon is divided into triangles by drawing lines from its centre to each vertex. What is the size of each angle at the centre of the hexagon?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 45°
2. [ ] B) 60°
3. [ ] C) 72°
4. [ ] D) 90°
5. [ ] E) 120°

**Solution:**
> • A regular hexagon has 6 equal sides and 6 vertices
• Drawing lines from the centre to each vertex creates 6 identical triangles
• The angles at the centre form a complete rotation around a point, which equals 360°
• Each central angle = 360° ÷ 6 = 60°
• Therefore, the answer is B because each angle at the centre measures 60°

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e0390c49-431a-47f3-a08a-bc4324c2fb10`

**Question:**
> A clock shows 3:00. What is the angle between the hour hand and the minute hand?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 60°
2. [ ] B) 90°
3. [ ] C) 120°
4. [ ] D) 180°
5. [ ] E) 45°

**Solution:**
> • At 3:00, the minute hand points at 12 and the hour hand points at 3
• A clock is divided into 12 hours, so each hour represents 360° ÷ 12 = 30°
• From 12 to 3 is 3 hours, so the angle is 3 × 30° = 90°
• Therefore, the answer is B because the angle between the hands is 90°

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d6375850-baec-4fb5-acdc-3cc3ce900298`

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 35m
2. [ ] B) 70m
3. [ ] C) 50m
4. [ ] D) 250m
5. [ ] E) 60m

**Solution:**
> • Perimeter of a rectangle = 2 × (length + width)
• Perimeter = 2 × (25 + 10)
• Perimeter = 2 × 35 = 70 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the perimeter is 70m

**ID:** `d497fea4-3209-4ca1-b66c-d691fa9d94dc`

1. [ ] A) 16cm

4. [ ] D) 4cm
5. [ ] E) 12cm

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 60
2. [ ] B) 70
3. [ ] C) 80
4. [ ] D) 90
5. [ ] E) 110

**Solution:**
> • The sum of all angles in any triangle equals 180°
• We have: 65° + 45° + x° = 180°
• Simplifying: 110° + x° = 180°
• Solving for x: x° = 180° - 110° = 70°
• Therefore, the answer is B because the missing angle must be 70° to make the angle sum equal to 180°

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Mathematics - Fractions & Mixed Numbers - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `1e14075b-ad1a-4cc7-9877-5e171efd8cd8`

**Question:**
> A librarian sorted books and found that 5/12 were fiction and 1/3 were non-fiction. What fraction of the books were either fiction or non-fiction?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6/15
2. [ ] B) 3/4
3. [ ] C) 8/12
4. [ ] D) 6/12
5. [ ] E) 9/12

**Solution:**
> • Find a common denominator for 5/12 and 1/3. The common denominator is 12.
• Convert 1/3 to twelfths: 1/3 = 4/12
• Add the fractions: 5/12 + 4/12 = 9/12
• Simplify: 9/12 = 3/4
• Therefore, the answer is B because 3/4 of the books were either fiction or non-fiction.

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `abbe4bbb-577f-4f38-922f-8aa5d0115725`

**Question:**
> A cyclist rode 3/4 of the distance to the finish line in the morning and 1/6 of the distance in the afternoon. What fraction of the total distance has the cyclist completed?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4/10
2. [ ] B) 11/12
3. [ ] C) 5/6
4. [ ] D) 4/6
5. [ ] E) 11/10

**Solution:**
> • Find a common denominator for 3/4 and 1/6. The LCD is 12.
• Convert: 3/4 = 9/12 and 1/6 = 2/12
• Add: 9/12 + 2/12 = 11/12
• Therefore, the answer is B because the cyclist has completed 11/12 of the total distance.

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0f9f17dc-eacc-44cf-a21c-bbfd4903af5b`

**Question:**
> A gardener planted flowers in rows. Each row requires 2 2/5 metres of space. If the gardener has 16 4/5 metres of garden bed available, how many complete rows can be planted?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 7
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 9

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 16 4/5 = 84/5 and 2 2/5 = 12/5
• Divide total space by space per row: 84/5 ÷ 12/5 = 84/5 × 5/12 = 84/12 = 7
• Therefore, the answer is B because 7 complete rows can be planted

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e357f667-994b-4807-8169-2e1073599b29`

**Question:**
> A scientist measured that a bacteria culture grew from 1 1/8 grams to 4 3/4 grams. By what factor did the bacteria culture multiply?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3 2/3
2. [ ] B) 4 2/9
3. [ ] C) 3 5/8
4. [ ] D) 4 1/9
5. [ ] E) 3 1/2

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 4 3/4 = 19/4 and 1 1/8 = 9/8
• Divide final amount by initial amount: 19/4 ÷ 9/8 = 19/4 × 8/9 = 152/36
• Simplify: 152/36 = 38/9
• Convert to mixed number: 38 ÷ 9 = 4 remainder 2, so 38/9 = 4 2/9
• Therefore, the answer is B because the bacteria culture multiplied by a factor of 4 2/9

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d9d06c27-83e2-496a-984c-091f3921e732`

**Question:**
> A video game developer found that 3/8 of players completed Level 1, and of those players, 2/3 went on to complete Level 2. What fraction of all players completed Level 2?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5/11
2. [ ] B) 1/4
3. [ ] C) 2/8
4. [ ] D) 6/24
5. [ ] E) 5/8

**Solution:**
> • To find the fraction of all players who completed Level 2, multiply the fraction who completed Level 1 by the fraction of those who went on to complete Level 2
• Calculate: 3/8 × 2/3 = (3 × 2)/(8 × 3) = 6/24
• Simplify: 6/24 = 1/4 (divide both numerator and denominator by 6)
• Therefore, the answer is B because 1/4 of all players completed Level 2

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Mathematics - Statistics & Data Interpretation - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `f6fc3046-d679-453b-8960-9e2800e09b3e`

**Question:**
> The table shows the number of medals won by five countries at a sports competition:

Country A: 18 medals
Country B: 25 medals
Country C: 14 medals
Country D: 22 medals
Country E: 16 medals

What is the range of medals won?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 11
2. [ ] B) 19
3. [ ] C) 25
4. [ ] D) 14
5. [ ] E) 22

**Solution:**
> • The range is found by subtracting the smallest value from the largest value
• Identify the highest number of medals: 25 (Country B)
• Identify the lowest number of medals: 14 (Country C)
• Range = 25 - 14 = 11
• Therefore, the answer is A because the range of medals won is 11

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `45406b51-fdec-423b-9d5e-f269b1e3a227`

**Question:**
> A cinema recorded the number of tickets sold for evening screenings over 9 consecutive days: 58, 43, 67, 58, 72, 58, 61, 49, 58. The cinema manager wants to know the median number of tickets sold. What is the median?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 58
2. [ ] B) 59
3. [ ] C) 61
4. [ ] D) 67
5. [ ] E) 58.2

**Solution:**
> • First, arrange the data in ascending order: 43, 49, 58, 58, 58, 58, 61, 67, 72
• With 9 values, the median is the 5th value (the middle position)
• The 5th value in the ordered list is 58
• Therefore, the answer is A because the median number of tickets sold is 58

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0b964a7a-5d4d-487f-99cf-3ddedfa4776a`

**Question:**
> The bar graph shows the daily temperature (in °C) recorded in a city over one week. On how many days was the temperature above the mean temperature for the week?

Monday: 18°C, Tuesday: 22°C, Wednesday: 20°C, Thursday: 25°C, Friday: 19°C, Saturday: 24°C, Sunday: 20°C

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2
2. [ ] B) 3
3. [ ] C) 4
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 6

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the mean temperature: (18 + 22 + 20 + 25 + 19 + 24 + 20) ÷ 7 = 148 ÷ 7 = 21.14°C (approximately)
• Count days above 21.14°C: Tuesday (22°C), Thursday (25°C), and Saturday (24°C)
• Therefore, the answer is B because 3 days had temperatures above the mean

5. [ ] E) 42

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 78 g
2. [ ] B) 85 g
3. [ ] C) 88 g
4. [ ] D) 87 g
5. [ ] E) 92 g

**Solution:**

• Count the frequency of each mass: 73 (once), 78 (once), 85 (three times), 88 (once), 92 (once), 95 (once), 101 (once)
• The mass 85 g appears 3 times, which is more than any other value
• Therefore, the answer is B because 85 g is the mode

1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 13
3. [ ] C) 12
4. [ ] D) 78
5. [ ] E) 7

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9d7371cf-6a56-404c-8967-fa2c28eff48c`

**Question:**
> A train travels 180 kilometers in 2 hours. At this same speed, how long will it take to travel 315 kilometers?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2.5 hours
2. [ ] B) 3.5 hours
3. [ ] C) 4 hours
4. [ ] D) 90 hours
5. [ ] E) 3 hours

**Solution:**
> • First, find the speed: 180 ÷ 2 = 90 kilometers per hour
• Then, find the time for 315 km: 315 ÷ 90 = 3.5 hours
• Therefore, the answer is B because the train travels at 90 km/h and will take 3.5 hours to cover 315 kilometers

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `01854aa3-6e33-4398-b2d5-0c1517d42d1e`

**Question:**
> A swimming pool is being filled with water at a rate of 450 litres per hour. After 3 hours, the pool is 40% full. How many more hours will it take to completely fill the pool?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3 hours
2. [ ] B) 4.5 hours
3. [ ] C) 5 hours
4. [ ] D) 7.5 hours
5. [ ] E) 10.5 hours

**Solution:**
> • Water filled in 3 hours = 450 × 3 = 1350 litres
• If 1350 litres = 40% of pool, then full capacity = 1350 ÷ 0.40 = 3375 litres
• Remaining water needed = 3375 - 1350 = 2025 litres
• Time to fill remaining = 2025 ÷ 450 = 4.5 hours
• Therefore, the answer is B because it will take 4.5 more hours to completely fill the pool

4. [ ] D) 13
5. [ ] E) 288

4. [ ] D) 640
5. [ ] E) 2400

• Then, find toys produced per day: 80 × 8 = 640 toys per day
• Finally, find toys produced in 5 days: 640 × 5 = 3200 toys

**Question:**
> A zoo keeper feeds the penguins f fish each morning. Find the value of: 4f - 6 when f = 9

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 30
2. [ ] B) 42
3. [ ] C) 36
4. [ ] D) 27
5. [ ] E) 48

**Solution:**
> • Substitute f = 9 into the expression 4f - 6
• Calculate: 4(9) - 6 = 36 - 6 = 30
• Therefore, the answer is A because when f = 9, the expression 4f - 6 equals 30

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `84e0f4ce-b304-487c-9a5b-781ffcfd6f9b`

**Question:**
> A computer programmer debugs lines of code each day. If she debugs 7 lines on Monday and then debugs d lines each day for the next 4 days, the total number of lines debugged is 47. Solve for d: 7 + 4d = 47

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8
2. [ ] B) 10
3. [ ] C) 12
4. [ ] D) 13
5. [ ] E) 15

**Solution:**
> • Start with the equation: 7 + 4d = 47
• Subtract 7 from both sides: 4d = 40
• Divide both sides by 4: d = 10
• Therefore, the answer is B because the programmer debugs 10 lines of code each day for the next 4 days

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `1d577b66-c0fb-459b-9e41-866dc094c81b`

**Question:**
> A museum charges an entry fee plus an additional cost per exhibition visited. If visiting 4 exhibitions costs $26 and visiting 7 exhibitions costs $38, what is the entry fee in dollars? (Let the entry fee be f and the cost per exhibition be e, so f + 4e = 26 and f + 7e = 38)

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $6
2. [ ] B) $10
3. [ ] C) $8
4. [ ] D) $12
5. [ ] E) $14

**Solution:**
> • From the two equations: f + 4e = 26 and f + 7e = 38
• Subtract the first equation from the second: (f + 7e) - (f + 4e) = 38 - 26
• This gives: 3e = 12, so e = 4
• Substitute e = 4 into f + 4e = 26: f + 4(4) = 26, so f + 16 = 26
• Therefore f = 10
• Therefore, the answer is B because the entry fee is $10

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `8fbf8065-e1b9-4d2b-b0ab-9b0749de492b`

**Question:**
> A photographer charges a booking fee plus an hourly rate. If a 3-hour session costs $165 and a 7-hour session costs $285, what is the hourly rate? Let h represent the hourly rate and solve: 3h + b = 165 and 7h + b = 285, where b is the booking fee.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $25
2. [ ] B) $30
3. [ ] C) $35
4. [ ] D) $40
5. [ ] E) $45

**Solution:**
> • Subtract the first equation from the second: (7h + b) - (3h + b) = 285 - 165
• Simplify: 4h = 120
• Divide both sides by 4: h = 30
• Therefore, the answer is B because the hourly rate is $30

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `949aba0b-662a-4535-b4f4-533717ee65d7`

**Question:**
> A trapezoid-shaped window has parallel sides of length 8 metres and 12 metres. The perpendicular distance between these parallel sides is 5 metres. What is the area of the window?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 40 square metres
2. [ ] B) 50 square metres
3. [ ] C) 60 square metres
4. [ ] D) 100 square metres
5. [ ] E) 25 square metres

**Solution:**
> • The area of a trapezoid is calculated using the formula: Area = ½ × (sum of parallel sides) × height
• Sum of parallel sides = 8 + 12 = 20 metres
• Area = ½ × 20 × 5 = 10 × 5 = 50 square metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of the trapezoid-shaped window is 50 square metres

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c98ae3b4-7efd-402e-8e7d-e31de3743b10`

**Question:**
> A rectangular poster is 30cm wide and 50cm long. What is its area?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 80 square centimetres
2. [ ] B) 1500 square centimetres
3. [ ] C) 160 square centimetres
4. [ ] D) 750 square centimetres
5. [ ] E) 1000 square centimetres

**Solution:**
> • Area of a rectangle = length × width
• Area = 50cm × 30cm = 1500 square centimetres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area is calculated by multiplying the length and width together.

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `ce1bed87-4df6-44a0-a2e3-1d9730d92722`

**Question:**
> A rhombus-shaped kite has one interior angle measuring 120°. What is the measure of the smallest angle in the rhombus?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 30°
2. [ ] B) 60°
3. [ ] C) 45°
4. [ ] D) 75°
5. [ ] E) 50°

**Solution:**
> • In a rhombus, opposite angles are equal and adjacent angles are supplementary (sum to 180°)
• If one angle is 120°, then the adjacent angle = 180° - 120° = 60°
• The four angles are: 120°, 60°, 120°, 60°
• Therefore, the answer is B because the smallest angle measures 60°

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2b554589-7132-4fb4-bad0-ab7f176b5579`

**Question:**
> A cube-shaped gift box has edges that are each 6cm long. How many faces does the cube have?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 10
5. [ ] E) 12

**Solution:**
> • A cube is a three-dimensional shape with square faces
• By definition, a cube has 6 faces (top, bottom, front, back, left, right)
• The length of the edges does not change the number of faces
• Therefore, the answer is B because a cube always has 6 faces

**Question:**
> A circular trampoline has a diameter of 4 metres. What is the radius of the trampoline?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8 metres
2. [ ] B) 2 metres
3. [ ] C) 4 metres
4. [ ] D) 1 metre
5. [ ] E) 6 metres

**Solution:**
> • The radius of a circle is half of its diameter
• Radius = Diameter ÷ 2
• Radius = 4 ÷ 2 = 2 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the radius is half the diameter

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Mathematics - Statistics & Data Interpretation - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `7893624f-598e-4424-9f03-d40ab7a70fe1`

**Question:**
> A pie chart shows how 240 students at a school chose their favourite season:

Spring: 25%, Summer: 35%, Autumn: 15%, Winter: 25%

How many more students chose Summer than Autumn?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 20
2. [ ] B) 48
3. [ ] C) 36
4. [ ] D) 84
5. [ ] E) 60

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the number of students who chose Summer: 35% of 240 = 0.35 × 240 = 84 students
• Next, calculate the number of students who chose Autumn: 15% of 240 = 0.15 × 240 = 36 students
• Find the difference: 84 - 36 = 48 students
• Therefore, the answer is B because 48 more students chose Summer than Autumn

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2a565e87-dde1-4387-b124-df7cfc1c17b6`

**Question:**
> A weather station recorded the rainfall (in millimetres) over 9 consecutive days: 12, 8, 15, 8, 22, 18, 8, 25, 14. What is the difference between the median rainfall and the mode rainfall?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6 mm
2. [ ] B) 6.5 mm
3. [ ] C) 7 mm
4. [ ] D) 8 mm
5. [ ] E) 14 mm

**Solution:**
> • First, arrange the data in order: 8, 8, 8, 12, 14, 15, 18, 22, 25
• The median is the middle value (5th out of 9 numbers) = 14 mm
• The mode is the most frequently occurring value = 8 mm (appears 3 times)
• The difference = 14 - 8 = 6 mm
• Therefore, the answer is A because the difference between the median (14 mm) and mode (8 mm) is 6 mm

---

What is the range of the number of games sold during the week?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 18
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 28
4. [ ] D) 34
5. [ ] E) 52

**Solution:**
> • Range = highest value − lowest value
• Highest number of games sold = 52 (Friday)
• Lowest number of games sold = 28 (Tuesday)
• Range = 52 − 28 = 24
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range is the difference between the maximum and minimum values

Game 2: 24 points
Game 3: 15 points
Game 4: 22 points
Game 5: 18 points
Game 6: 30 points
Game 7: 18 points
Game 8: 26 points
Game 9: 21 points

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 0
2. [ ] B) 3
3. [ ] C) 4
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 6

**Solution:**
> • First, arrange the scores in order: 15, 18, 18, 18, 21, 22, 24, 26, 30
• The mode is the most frequently occurring value: 18 appears 3 times, which is more than any other value, so mode = 18
• The median is the middle value: with 9 numbers, the middle value is the 5th number = 21
• The difference between mode and median = 21 - 18 = 3
• Therefore, the answer is B because the difference is 3 points

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/diagnostic - Mathematics - Statistics & Data Interpretation - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `82176765-c38b-4d6d-aa31-372c120861cf`

**Question:**
> A science class recorded the daily maximum temperatures (in °C) during an experiment over 7 days: 22, 19, 25, 22, 28, 22, 21. What is the median temperature?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 21°C
2. [ ] B) 22°C
3. [ ] C) 23°C
4. [ ] D) 25°C
5. [ ] E) 28°C

**Solution:**
> • To find the median, first arrange the temperatures in order from lowest to highest: 19, 21, 22, 22, 22, 25, 28
• Since there are 7 values (an odd number), the median is the middle value, which is the 4th value
• The 4th value in the ordered list is 22
• Therefore, the answer is B because the median temperature is 22°C

**ID:** `fab995b7-be17-46f4-8777-5d16507b4e5c`

**Question:**
> A gaming tournament tracked the number of wins achieved by 8 players during the qualifying round: 7, 12, 9, 15, 9, 11, 9, 14. The tournament organizers want to report the most frequently occurring number of wins. What statistic should they use, and what is its value?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) Mean: 10.75
2. [ ] B) Mode: 9
3. [ ] C) Median: 10
4. [ ] D) Range: 8
5. [ ] E) Mode: 11

**Solution:**
> • The question asks for the most frequently occurring value, which is the mode
• List the data: 7, 12, 9, 15, 9, 11, 9, 14
• Count the frequency of each number: 7 appears once, 9 appears three times, 11 appears once, 12 appears once, 14 appears once, 15 appears once
• The mode is 9 because it appears most frequently (3 times)
• Therefore, the answer is B because the mode is 9

• Therefore, the answer is B because 92 is the mode (appears on Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday)

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `bb23427a-df8a-4cbf-9d40-98c38e91ab8e`

**Question:**
> A video game developer designs levels with increasing difficulty. The number of obstacles in each level is given by the formula 4(L + 2) - 5, where L is the level number. If a particular level has 23 obstacles, solve for L.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3
2. [ ] B) 5
3. [ ] C) 7
4. [ ] D) 4
5. [ ] E) 6

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: 4(L + 2) - 5 = 23
• Add 5 to both sides: 4(L + 2) = 28
• Divide both sides by 4: L + 2 = 7
• Subtract 2 from both sides: L = 5
• Therefore, the answer is B because the level number is 5

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `92c4a120-d709-4269-9524-95cccab36091`

**Question:**
> A rectangular smartphone screen has a length of 15 cm and a width of 8 cm. A protective film is placed diagonally across the screen from one corner to the opposite corner. What is the length of this diagonal? (Use the Pythagorean theorem: a² + b² = c²)

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 23 cm
2. [ ] B) 17 cm
3. [ ] C) 19 cm
4. [ ] D) 15 cm
5. [ ] E) 21 cm

**Solution:**
> • Using the Pythagorean theorem where a = 15 cm and b = 8 cm
• Calculate: 15² + 8² = c²
• 225 + 64 = c²
• 289 = c²
• c = √289 = 17 cm
• Therefore, the answer is B because the diagonal measures 17 cm

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9ceb6561-1788-48d5-b02c-6c5db6d020d9`

**Question:**
> A rectangular flag is folded in half along its diagonal, creating two congruent triangles. If the flag has a length of 18 cm and a width of 12 cm, what is the area of one of the triangular halves?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 54 cm²
2. [ ] B) 108 cm²
3. [ ] C) 216 cm²
4. [ ] D) 30 cm²
5. [ ] E) 180 cm²

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the area of the rectangular flag: Area = length × width = 18 × 12 = 216 cm²
• When folded along the diagonal, the rectangle is divided into two congruent triangles
• Each triangle has half the area of the rectangle: 216 ÷ 2 = 108 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because each triangular half has an area of 108 cm²

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9895e6a3-e5b1-4b7f-8381-387261a9cd40`

**Question:**
> A circular clock face has a radius of 14 centimetres. What is the diameter of the clock face?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7cm
2. [ ] B) 28cm
3. [ ] C) 21cm
4. [ ] D) 14cm
5. [ ] E) 42cm

**Solution:**
> • The diameter of a circle is twice the radius
• Diameter = 2 × radius = 2 × 14cm = 28cm
• Therefore, the answer is B because the diameter is 28cm

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e94339e3-cff4-47f7-a848-52bd162c4ede`

**Question:**
> A triangular pizza slice has three angles. Two of the angles measure 70° and 60°. What is the measure of the third angle?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 40°
2. [ ] B) 50°
3. [ ] C) 60°
4. [ ] D) 70°
5. [ ] E) 80°

**Solution:**
> • The sum of all angles in any triangle is always 180°
• Two angles measure 70° and 60°, so their sum is 70° + 60° = 130°
• The third angle = 180° - 130° = 50°
• Therefore, the answer is B because the third angle must be 50°

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `12618633-0144-4b62-958e-3fde14e173d6`

**Question:**
> A triangular park has a perimeter of 48 metres. Two of its sides are equal in length, each measuring 15 metres. If the area of the park is 108 square metres, what is the height of the triangle when the third side is taken as the base?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 10 metres
2. [ ] B) 12 metres
3. [ ] C) 14 metres
4. [ ] D) 18 metres
5. [ ] E) 9 metres

**Solution:**
> • First, find the length of the third side (base): Perimeter = 48m, so base = 48 - 15 - 15 = 18 metres
• Use the area formula for triangles: Area = ½ × base × height
• Substitute known values: 108 = ½ × 18 × height
• Simplify: 108 = 9 × height
• Solve for height: height = 108 ÷ 9 = 12 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the height of the triangle is 12 metres

---

Team Red: 52 goals
Team Blue: 48 goals
Team Green: 61 goals
Team Yellow: 45 goals
Team Orange: 54 goals

What is the range of goals scored?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 13
2. [ ] B) 16
3. [ ] C) 52
4. [ ] D) 48
5. [ ] E) 54

**Solution:**
> • The range is calculated by subtracting the lowest value from the highest value
• Highest number of goals: 61 (Team Green)
• Lowest number of goals: 45 (Team Yellow)
• Range = 61 - 45 = 16
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range of goals scored is 16

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Mathematics - Fractions & Mixed Numbers - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `83ed2776-fdd4-4b47-988a-34fdffec075b`

**Question:**
> A robotics team used 5 1/6 kilograms of metal for the frame and 2 3/4 kilograms of metal for the wheels. How much metal did they use in total?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7 4/10 kg
2. [ ] B) 7 11/12 kg
3. [ ] C) 7 4/6 kg
4. [ ] D) 8 1/12 kg
5. [ ] E) 7 7/10 kg

**Solution:**
> • Add the whole numbers: 5 + 2 = 7
• Add the fractions: 1/6 + 3/4. Find common denominator (12): 1/6 = 2/12 and 3/4 = 9/12
• Add the fractions: 2/12 + 9/12 = 11/12
• Total: 7 + 11/12 = 7 11/12 kilograms
• Therefore, the answer is B because the robotics team used 7 11/12 kilograms of metal in total

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `8d79ad0e-a487-42f0-b284-fd87b4a6aea9`

**Question:**
> A painter mixed 3 1/4 litres of blue paint with 2 3/4 litres of yellow paint to create green paint. How many litres of green paint did the painter make?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5 1/2 litres
2. [ ] B) 6 litres
3. [ ] C) 5 4/8 litres
4. [ ] D) 6 1/4 litres
5. [ ] E) 5 2/4 litres

**Solution:**
> • Add the whole numbers: 3 + 2 = 5
• Add the fractions: 1/4 + 3/4 = 4/4 = 1
• Combine: 5 + 1 = 6 litres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the painter made 6 litres of green paint

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0bc603a0-a177-4047-8eb8-cd2b3f2adaeb`

**Question:**
> A archaeologist excavated artifacts from three different layers of soil. The first layer was 1 5/6 metres deep, the second layer was 2 1/3 metres deep, and the third layer was 1 1/2 metres deep. What was the total depth excavated?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5 1/2 metres
2. [ ] B) 5 2/3 metres
3. [ ] C) 5 5/6 metres
4. [ ] D) 6 1/6 metres
5. [ ] E) 4 2/3 metres

**Solution:**
> • Add whole numbers: 1 + 2 + 1 = 4
• Convert fractions to common denominator of 6: 5/6 + 1/3 + 1/2 = 5/6 + 2/6 + 3/6
• Add fractions: 5/6 + 2/6 + 3/6 = 10/6 = 1 4/6 = 1 2/3
• Add whole number and fraction: 4 + 1 2/3 = 5 2/3
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total depth excavated was 5 2/3 metres

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `8398b3a6-7e85-4eee-876c-d8e94167ce77`

**Question:**
> A construction worker needs to cut a steel beam that is 9 1/3 metres long into pieces that are each 1 1/4 metres long. How many complete pieces can be cut from the beam?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 7
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 9
5. [ ] E) 10

**Solution:**
> • Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: 9 1/3 = 28/3 and 1 1/4 = 5/4
• Divide the total length by the piece length: (28/3) ÷ (5/4) = (28/3) × (4/5) = 112/15
• Convert to mixed number: 112 ÷ 15 = 7 remainder 7, so 112/15 = 7 7/15
• Therefore, the answer is B because only 7 complete pieces can be cut (we ignore the partial piece)

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `0d80d555-3857-445a-9865-c0d3ae91161e`

**Question:**
> A music teacher divided a practice session into sections. Warm-up took 1/6 of the time, technique practice took 1/3 of the time, and performance took 1/2 of the time. What fraction of the practice session is accounted for?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5/6
2. [ ] B) 1
3. [ ] C) 11/12
4. [ ] D) 6/11
5. [ ] E) 5/11

**Solution:**
> • Find a common denominator for 1/6, 1/3, and 1/2. The LCD is 6.
• Convert each fraction: 1/6 = 1/6, 1/3 = 2/6, 1/2 = 3/6
• Add the fractions: 1/6 + 2/6 + 3/6 = 6/6 = 1
• Therefore, the answer is B because the entire practice session (1 whole) is accounted for.

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Mathematics - Applied Word Problems - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `40599f36-59c3-48cc-9dd0-4adce0f01ecb`

**Question:**
> A parking garage charges $4.50 for the first hour and $2.25 for each additional hour. How much does it cost to park for 5 hours?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $11.25
2. [ ] B) $13.50
3. [ ] C) $15.75
4. [ ] D) $18.00
5. [ ] E) $22.50

**Solution:**
> • First hour costs $4.50
• Additional hours = 5 - 1 = 4 hours
• Cost for additional hours = 4 × $2.25 = $9.00
• Total cost = $4.50 + $9.00 = $13.50
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total parking cost for 5 hours is $13.50

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c7772475-9ded-4de4-8fe3-87e6391b73d9`

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 216 km
2. [ ] B) 288 km
3. [ ] C) 240 km
4. [ ] D) 200 km
5. [ ] E) 260 km

**Solution:**
> • First, find the speed: 180 ÷ 2.5 = 72 kilometers per hour
• Then multiply the speed by 4 hours: 72 × 4 = 288 kilometers
• Therefore, the answer is B because the train will travel 288 km in 4 hours at the same speed

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5/8
2. [ ] B) 3/8
3. [ ] C) 1/2
4. [ ] D) 2/8
5. [ ] E) 1/4

**Solution:**
> • Tom eats 3 slices and his sister eats 2 slices, so total eaten = 3 + 2 = 5 slices
• Pizza has 8 slices total, so slices left = 8 - 5 = 3 slices
• Therefore, the answer is B because 3 slices out of 8 equals 3/8 of the pizza

4. [ ] D) $2.50
5. [ ] E) $3.50

**Options:**

2. [ ] B) $354
3. [ ] C) $318
4. [ ] D) $84
5. [ ] E) $438

**Solution:**
> • Labor cost = $45 × 6 hours = $270
• Paint cost = $28 × 3 cans = $84
• Total cost = $270 + $84 = $354
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total cost includes both labor and materials

3. [ ] C) 9:30 PM
4. [ ] D) 9:00 PM
5. [ ] E) 10:00 PM

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 25
2. [ ] B) 35
3. [ ] C) 40
4. [ ] D) 45
5. [ ] E) 50

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate money from adult tickets: 45 × $8 = $360
• Then, find money from child tickets: $535 - $360 = $175
• Finally, divide by child ticket price: $175 ÷ $5 = 35 child tickets
• Therefore, the answer is B because 35 child tickets were sold

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 150 kg
2. [ ] B) 180 kg
3. [ ] C) 187.5 kg
4. [ ] D) 195 kg
5. [ ] E) 225 kg

**Solution:**
> • First, find how many full boxes can be made: 450 ÷ 36 = 12.5, so 12 full boxes (we only count full boxes)
• Each full box weighs 15 kg, so total weight = 12 × 15 = 180 kg
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 full boxes at 15 kg each equals 180 kilograms

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Mathematics - Algebra & Equation Solving - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b7db40fc-61db-4604-8c4f-61a7a065c934`

**Question:**
> A factory produces toy cars. The number of cars made each hour is given by the expression 3h + 5, where h is the number of hours. Find the value when h = 4.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12
2. [ ] B) 17
3. [ ] C) 15
4. [ ] D) 20
5. [ ] E) 9

**Solution:**
> • Substitute h = 4 into the expression 3h + 5
• Calculate: 3(4) + 5 = 12 + 5 = 17
• Therefore, the answer is B because when h = 4, the factory produces 17 toy cars

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `45d9f818-274b-40ab-bac7-2204d5250e27`

**Question:**
> Solve for x: 4(x + 5) - 7 = 2x + 9

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2
2. [ ] B) -2
3. [ ] C) 7
4. [ ] D) 3
5. [ ] E) -7

**Solution:**
> • Expand the left side: 4x + 20 - 7 = 2x + 9
• Simplify the left side: 4x + 13 = 2x + 9
• Subtract 2x from both sides: 2x + 13 = 9
• Subtract 13 from both sides: 2x = -4
• Divide both sides by 2: x = -2
• Therefore, the answer is B because x = -2

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `40c12fd2-8c2c-4d38-954c-c86d6262a5cb`

**Question:**
> A marine biologist studies dolphin pods. The number of dolphins spotted increases each week. If the expression 5(w + 3) - 7 represents the total number of dolphins after w weeks, solve for w when the total reaches 43 dolphins.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 7
3. [ ] C) 10
4. [ ] D) 4
5. [ ] E) 6

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: 5(w + 3) - 7 = 43
• Expand the brackets: 5w + 15 - 7 = 43
• Simplify: 5w + 8 = 43
• Subtract 8 from both sides: 5w = 35
• Divide by 5: w = 7
• Therefore, the answer is B because w = 7 weeks

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9a9d3b10-c274-47ae-9684-29cf6ebfd9b2`

**Question:**
> A musician practiced for 3/8 of an hour in the morning and 1/8 of an hour in the evening. What fraction of an hour did she practice in total?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4/16
2. [ ] B) 4/8
3. [ ] C) 3/16
4. [ ] D) 2/8
5. [ ] E) 4/64

**Solution:**
> • Both fractions have the same denominator (8), so we can add them directly.
• Add the numerators: 3/8 + 1/8 = (3 + 1)/8 = 4/8
• Therefore, the answer is B because the musician practiced 4/8 of an hour in total.

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `25b676ec-43f5-4c5a-b35b-b03338b9d0dc`

**Question:**
> A chocolatier mixed 2 3/4 kilograms of dark chocolate with 1 1/3 kilograms of milk chocolate. If she then divided the mixture equally into 6 boxes, how many kilograms of chocolate did each box contain?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 11/16 kg
2. [ ] B) 49/72 kg
3. [ ] C) 2/3 kg
4. [ ] D) 4 1/12 kg
5. [ ] E) 3/4 kg

**Solution:**
> • First, add the two amounts: 2 3/4 + 1 1/3
• Convert to improper fractions: 11/4 + 4/3
• Find common denominator (12): 33/12 + 16/12 = 49/12 kg total
• Divide by 6: 49/12 ÷ 6 = 49/12 × 1/6 = 49/72 kg
• Therefore, the answer is B because each box contains 49/72 kilograms of chocolate

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `05edf441-2d08-40cc-afbb-55b90740e353`

**Question:**
> A carpenter cut a wooden plank into two pieces. The first piece was 4 2/5 metres long. If the original plank was 7 1/10 metres long, how long was the second piece?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2 7/10 metres
2. [ ] B) 2 7/5 metres
3. [ ] C) 3 1/2 metres
4. [ ] D) 3 7/10 metres
5. [ ] E) 2 3/5 metres

**Solution:**
> • Subtract the first piece from the original length: 7 1/10 - 4 2/5
• Convert to common denominator: 7 1/10 - 4 4/10
• Subtract whole numbers: 7 - 4 = 3
• Subtract fractions: 1/10 - 4/10 requires borrowing. Convert 3 to 2 11/10
• Now calculate: 2 11/10 - 4/10 = 2 7/10
• Therefore, the answer is A because the second piece is 2 7/10 metres long

3. [ ] C) 6 7/8
4. [ ] D) 5 6/8
5. [ ] E) 4 7/8

**Solution:**
