### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `885270d1-8329-4969-b0a3-381fda9c81a3`

**Question:**
> A rectangular piece of paper measuring 24 cm by 18 cm has four identical squares cut from its corners. If each square has a side length of 3 cm, what is the perimeter of the remaining shape?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 84 cm
2. [ ] B) 108 cm
3. [ ] C) 96 cm
4. [ ] D) 102 cm
5. [ ] E) 90 cm

**Solution:**
> • Original rectangle has perimeter = 2(24 + 18) = 84 cm, but this changes when corners are cut
• When a square is cut from a corner, we remove 2 sides of length 3 cm from the perimeter, but add 2 new sides of length 3 cm
• Each corner cut removes sides totaling 6 cm and adds sides totaling 6 cm, creating an indentation
• The new perimeter = original perimeter + (additional perimeter from cuts) = 84 + 4(2 × 3) = 84 + 24 = 108 cm
• Alternatively: count all outer edges: top has 24 - 3 - 3 + 3 + 3 = 24 cm, similarly for all sides, plus the 8 new edges of 3 cm each = 24 + 24 + 18 + 18 + 24 = 108 cm
• Therefore, the answer is B because cutting corners adds extra edges that increase the total perimeter to 108 cm

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `5a511ba2-4564-432c-b3b6-ffcee1d7fc9b`

**Question:**
> A rectangular soccer field has a length that is 3 times its width. If the perimeter of the field is 160 metres, what is the area of the field in square metres?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 1200
2. [ ] B) 1200
3. [ ] C) 800
4. [ ] D) 960
5. [ ] E) 600

**Solution:**
> • Let the width be w metres, then the length is 3w metres
• Perimeter = 2(length + width) = 2(3w + w) = 2(4w) = 8w
• Since perimeter = 160 metres: 8w = 160, so w = 20 metres
• Length = 3w = 3 × 20 = 60 metres
• Area = length × width = 60 × 20 = 1200 square metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of the rectangular field is 1200 square metres

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d0292ef3-8ed8-407c-bebf-a5b9e698f297`

**Question:**
> A trapezoid-shaped skateboard ramp has parallel sides of 8 metres and 14 metres. The perpendicular distance between these parallel sides is 5 metres. What is the area of the ramp?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 50 square metres
2. [ ] B) 55 square metres
3. [ ] C) 60 square metres
4. [ ] D) 70 square metres
5. [ ] E) 110 square metres

**Solution:**
> • The area of a trapezoid is calculated using the formula: Area = ½ × (sum of parallel sides) × height
• The parallel sides are 8 metres and 14 metres, so their sum is 8 + 14 = 22 metres
• Area = ½ × 22 × 5 = 11 × 5 = 55 square metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of the trapezoid-shaped ramp is 55 square metres

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `353eb796-9449-48f8-86ae-57f8e200c5c0`

**Question:**
> A square picture frame has sides that are each 20 centimetres long. What is the area of the picture frame?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 80 cm²
2. [ ] B) 400 cm²
3. [ ] C) 40 cm²
4. [ ] D) 200 cm²
5. [ ] E) 160 cm²

**Solution:**
> • A square has all sides equal in length
• Area of a square = side × side
• Area = 20 cm × 20 cm = 400 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of a square with sides of 20 cm is 400 square centimetres

**ID:** `406977e8-4c68-4378-8645-78ef21d571ca`

**Question:**
> A regular pentagon has 5 equal sides. If each side of the pentagon measures 7 centimetres, what is the perimeter of the pentagon?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12 cm
2. [ ] B) 35 cm
3. [ ] C) 28 cm
4. [ ] D) 42 cm
5. [ ] E) 21 cm

**Solution:**
> • A regular pentagon has 5 equal sides
• Each side measures 7 cm
• Perimeter = 5 × 7 = 35 cm
• Therefore, the answer is B because the perimeter is found by multiplying the number of sides by the length of each side

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `1a859a8f-28d3-4e04-96f6-4cc8e0492214`

**Question:**
> A table shows the number of bronze, silver, and gold medals won by five countries at a sports championship:

Country A: 8 gold, 12 silver, 15 bronze
Country B: 15 gold, 10 silver, 8 bronze
Country C: 6 gold, 14 silver, 18 bronze
Country D: 12 gold, 9 silver, 11 bronze
Country E: 9 gold, 15 silver, 13 bronze

What is the range of the total number of medals won by these countries?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 9
4. [ ] D) 35
5. [ ] E) 38

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate the total medals for each country:
• Country A: 8 + 12 + 15 = 35 medals
• Country B: 15 + 10 + 8 = 33 medals
• Country C: 6 + 14 + 18 = 38 medals
• Country D: 12 + 9 + 11 = 32 medals
• Country E: 9 + 15 + 13 = 37 medals
• Range = highest value - lowest value = 38 - 32 = 6
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range of total medals is 6

4. [ ] D) 71
5. [ ] E) 82

**Solution:**

• Smallest value: 58 books (Wednesday)
• Range = 82 - 58 = 24
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range of books borrowed is 24

5. [ ] E) 35

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Mathematics - Fractions & Mixed Numbers - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2f70a5ec-8549-42c0-a6de-7598050b10ae`

**Question:**
> A jeweller has a gold chain that is 7/12 of a metre long and a silver chain that is 5/12 of a metre long. What is the total length of both chains in metres?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 12/12
2. [ ] B) 1
3. [ ] C) 12/24
4. [ ] D) 2/3
5. [ ] E) 1 1/12

**Solution:**
> • The denominators are already the same (12), so we can add directly
• Add the numerators: 7/12 + 5/12 = (7 + 5)/12 = 12/12
• Simplify: 12/12 = 1
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total length is 1 metre

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `bb3d367c-062e-42dd-a483-6c649e761342`

**Question:**
> A mountaineer climbed 5 1/4 kilometres on the first day and 3 5/6 kilometres on the second day. How much further did she climb on the first day than on the second day?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 1 5/12 kilometres
2. [ ] B) 1 5/12 kilometres
3. [ ] C) 2 1/12 kilometres
4. [ ] D) 1 1/2 kilometres
5. [ ] E) 2 5/12 kilometres

**Solution:**
> • Convert to common denominator: 5 1/4 = 5 3/12 and 3 5/6 = 3 10/12
• Subtract: 5 3/12 - 3 10/12. Since 3/12 < 10/12, borrow 1 from 5: 4 15/12 - 3 10/12
• Subtract whole numbers: 4 - 3 = 1. Subtract fractions: 15/12 - 10/12 = 5/12
• Therefore, the answer is A because 5 1/4 - 3 5/6 = 1 5/12 kilometres

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `50f102c4-7d55-4ec4-bc8a-4549d5a3440b`

**Question:**
> A baker made 5 1/3 dozen cookies on Monday and sold 2 3/4 dozen. On Tuesday, she made twice as many cookies as she had left from Monday. How many dozen cookies did she make on Tuesday?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5 1/6 dozen
2. [ ] B) 5 1/2 dozen
3. [ ] C) 5 dozen
4. [ ] D) 10 1/3 dozen
5. [ ] E) 2 7/12 dozen

**Solution:**
> • First, find how many dozen cookies were left from Monday: 5 1/3 - 2 3/4
• Convert to improper fractions: 16/3 - 11/4
• Find common denominator (12): 64/12 - 33/12 = 31/12
• Convert to mixed number: 31/12 = 2 7/12 dozen left
• Tuesday's production is twice Monday's remainder: 2 × 2 7/12 = 2 × 31/12 = 62/12 = 5 2/12 = 5 1/6 dozen
• Therefore, the answer is A because the baker made 5 1/6 dozen cookies on Tuesday

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `7a566107-05ec-4b62-8dbb-693cc1ebee35`

**Question:**
> A train journey is divided into three segments. The first segment takes 2 1/6 hours, the second segment takes 1 3/4 hours, and the third segment takes 2 5/12 hours. What is the total journey time?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6 1/4 hours
2. [ ] B) 6 1/3 hours
3. [ ] C) 5 11/12 hours
4. [ ] D) 6 5/12 hours
5. [ ] E) 6 1/2 hours

**Solution:**
> • Add whole numbers: 2 + 1 + 2 = 5 hours
• Convert fractions to common denominator (12): 1/6 = 2/12, 3/4 = 9/12, 5/12 = 5/12
• Add fractions: 2/12 + 9/12 + 5/12 = 16/12 = 1 4/12 = 1 1/3
• Add whole number result to fraction result: 5 + 1 1/3 = 6 1/3 hours
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total journey time is 6 1/3 hours

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `42d792de-0ced-4192-99c2-56cd372db738`

**Question:**
> A meteorologist recorded that it rained 7 1/3 centimetres in the first week and 5 5/6 centimetres in the second week. How much more rain fell in the first week than in the second week?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 1 1/3 cm
2. [ ] B) 1 1/2 cm
3. [ ] C) 2 1/2 cm
4. [ ] D) 1 2/3 cm
5. [ ] E) 2 1/6 cm

**Solution:**
> • Subtract the two mixed numbers: 7 1/3 - 5 5/6
• Convert to common denominator: 7 2/6 - 5 5/6
• Since 2/6 < 5/6, borrow 1 from 7: 6 8/6 - 5 5/6
• Subtract whole numbers: 6 - 5 = 1
• Subtract fractions: 8/6 - 5/6 = 3/6 = 1/2
• Therefore, the answer is B because 7 1/3 - 5 5/6 = 1 1/2 cm

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Mathematics - Applied Word Problems - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9a5f15ce-9a13-4580-8ab5-8585562e0a1c`

**Question:**
> A nature reserve has a walking trail that is 3.6 kilometers long. A group of students walks the trail at an average speed of 4 kilometers per hour. If they start walking at 10:15 AM and take a 15-minute rest break halfway through, what time will they finish the trail?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 11:09 AM
2. [ ] B) 11:24 AM
3. [ ] C) 11:39 AM
4. [ ] D) 11:54 AM
5. [ ] E) 12:09 PM

**Solution:**
> • Time to walk 3.6 km at 4 km/h: 3.6 ÷ 4 = 0.9 hours = 54 minutes
• Add the 15-minute rest break: 54 + 15 = 69 minutes total
• Starting time is 10:15 AM, add 69 minutes: 10:15 + 69 minutes = 11:24 AM
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total time of 69 minutes (54 minutes walking + 15 minutes rest) added to 10:15 AM equals 11:24 AM

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `de520669-c13d-41cb-9022-f66a5186d509`

**Question:**
> A factory produces toy cars at a rate of 240 cars per hour. The factory operates for 6.5 hours on Monday and 5.25 hours on Tuesday. If the toys are packed into boxes of 18 cars each, how many full boxes can be made from Monday and Tuesday's production combined?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 130 boxes
2. [ ] B) 156 boxes
3. [ ] C) 162 boxes
4. [ ] D) 2808 boxes
5. [ ] E) 2916 boxes

**Solution:**
> • Monday production: 240 × 6.5 = 1560 cars
• Tuesday production: 240 × 5.25 = 1260 cars
• Total production: 1560 + 1260 = 2820 cars
• Number of full boxes: 2820 ÷ 18 = 156.666...
• Therefore, the answer is B because 156 full boxes can be made (we only count complete boxes)

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `f40f53ea-d2bc-4ba0-b0ff-bc28d3fbeee7`

**Question:**
> A bookstore is having a sale where all books are 30% off the original price. Sarah buys 4 books that originally cost $12 each. If she pays with a $50 note, how much change will she receive?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $15.60
2. [ ] B) $16.40
3. [ ] C) $33.60
4. [ ] D) $14.00
5. [ ] E) $2.00

**Solution:**
> • Original cost of 4 books: 4 × $12 = $48
• Discount amount: 30% of $48 = 0.30 × $48 = $14.40
• Sale price: $48 - $14.40 = $33.60
• Change from $50: $50 - $33.60 = $16.40
• Therefore, the answer is B because Sarah receives $16.40 in change

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `a068cdd5-c789-4c23-b794-b91790ce4bea`

**Question:**
> A printer can print 18 pages per minute. A student needs to print 5 copies of a 27-page report. If the printer takes 2 minutes to warm up before printing, how many minutes will the entire job take?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7.5 minutes
2. [ ] B) 9.5 minutes
3. [ ] C) 11.5 minutes
4. [ ] D) 7 minutes
5. [ ] E) 10 minutes

**Solution:**
> • Total pages to print: 5 copies × 27 pages = 135 pages
• Printing time: 135 pages ÷ 18 pages per minute = 7.5 minutes
• Total time: 2 minutes warm-up + 7.5 minutes printing = 9.5 minutes
• Therefore, the answer is B because the entire job takes 9.5 minutes including warm-up time.

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `fa8216b1-7334-4fa8-af33-5d840a540139`

**Question:**
> A museum charges $8 for adults and $5 for children. A family of 2 adults and 3 children visits the museum. If they pay with a $50 note, how much change do they receive?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $19
2. [ ] B) $31
3. [ ] C) $15
4. [ ] D) $21
5. [ ] E) $35

**Solution:**
> • Cost for adults: 2 × $8 = $16
• Cost for children: 3 × $5 = $15
• Total cost: $16 + $15 = $31
• Change received: $50 - $31 = $19
• Therefore, the answer is A because the family receives $19 in change

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `fa8eeae9-e53d-4337-8146-5e566744c775`

**Question:**
> A weather station records that 3258.4 millimetres of rainfall occurred over a year. To convert this measurement to metres for a scientific report, the value must be divided by 1000. What is 3258.4 ÷ 1000?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 32.584
2. [ ] B) 3.2584
3. [ ] C) 325.84
4. [ ] D) 0.32584
5. [ ] E) 32584

**Solution:**
> • To divide by 1000, move the decimal point 3 places to the left
• Starting with 3258.4, move the decimal point: 3258.4 → 325.84 → 32.584 → 3.2584
• Therefore, the answer is B because 3258.4 ÷ 1000 = 3.2584 metres

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `29632604-d135-4321-addc-6694ccebee53`

**Question:**
> A clockmaker measures three brass gears with masses of 6.45 grams, 8.7 grams, and 5.38 grams. After finding the total mass, she multiplies the result by 0.12 to calculate the copper content. What is the copper content in grams?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2.4636
2. [ ] B) 2.464
3. [ ] C) 24.636
4. [ ] D) 0.24636
5. [ ] E) 2.463

**Solution:**
> • First, add the masses: 6.45 + 8.7 + 5.38 = 20.53 grams
• Then multiply by 0.12: 20.53 × 0.12 = 2.4636
• Multiply as whole numbers: 2053 × 12 = 24636. Count decimal places: 2 + 2 = 4, so result is 2.4636
• Therefore, the answer is A because the copper content is 2.4636 grams

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Mathematics - Algebra & Equation Solving - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `077eb87d-9011-436d-be09-696c0a761358`

**Question:**
> A cyclist tracks the distance covered during a race. The distance in kilometers is given by the expression 7d + 2, where d represents the number of hours cycled. Find the value of this expression when d = 4.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 28
2. [ ] B) 30
3. [ ] C) 32
4. [ ] D) 34
5. [ ] E) 26

**Solution:**
> • Substitute d = 4 into the expression 7d + 2
• Calculate: 7(4) + 2 = 28 + 2 = 30
• Therefore, the answer is B because when d = 4, the expression equals 30 kilometers

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `828002ea-3301-419b-ac54-0227996b1a12`

**Question:**
> A chemist mixes two solutions in a laboratory. The first solution contains (2x + 7) milliliters and the second contains (5x - 3) milliliters. If the total volume is 46 milliliters, solve for x.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 7
4. [ ] D) 8
5. [ ] E) 4

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: (2x + 7) + (5x - 3) = 46
• Combine like terms: 2x + 5x + 7 - 3 = 46, which gives 7x + 4 = 46
• Subtract 4 from both sides: 7x = 42
• Divide both sides by 7: x = 6
• Therefore, the answer is B because x = 6

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9076c346-9472-48ed-b05b-5fab56e78de9`

**Question:**
> A baker decorates cupcakes for a party. Each cupcake needs 6 sprinkles. Find the value of: 6c + 4 when c = 5

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 15
2. [ ] B) 34
3. [ ] C) 30
4. [ ] D) 54
5. [ ] E) 26

**Solution:**
> • Substitute c = 5 into the expression: 6c + 4
• Calculate: 6(5) + 4 = 30 + 4 = 34
• Therefore, the answer is B because 6c + 4 = 34 when c = 5

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `fcda1593-0d9a-4c58-8ff6-6b01465be1a8`

**Question:**
> A game developer awards points to players. Each player earns 5 points per level completed. Find the value of: 5n + 7 when n = 6

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 42
2. [ ] B) 37
3. [ ] C) 32
4. [ ] D) 30
5. [ ] E) 18

**Solution:**
> • Substitute n = 6 into the expression 5n + 7
• Calculate: 5(6) + 7 = 30 + 7 = 37
• Therefore, the answer is B because when n = 6, the expression evaluates to 37

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d6447e5b-c188-49ae-9714-4a87182454d1`

**Question:**
> A bookstore owner calculates the total cost of ordering books. The cost in dollars is given by 4x + 3x - 9, where x is the number of boxes ordered. If the total cost is $33, how many boxes were ordered?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 7
4. [ ] D) 9
5. [ ] E) 12

**Solution:**
> • Set up the equation: 4x + 3x - 9 = 33
• Combine like terms: 7x - 9 = 33
• Add 9 to both sides: 7x = 42
• Divide both sides by 7: x = 6
• Therefore, the answer is B because 6 boxes were ordered

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Mathematics - Geometry & Spatial Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `6a37a4f1-4b75-4d69-bb79-5228f9499660`

**Question:**
> A rectangular classroom has a length of 12 metres and a width of 8 metres. What is the perimeter of the classroom?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 20 metres
2. [ ] B) 40 metres
3. [ ] C) 96 metres
4. [ ] D) 48 metres
5. [ ] E) 32 metres

**Solution:**
> • The perimeter of a rectangle is calculated using the formula: Perimeter = 2(length + width)
• Substituting the values: Perimeter = 2(12 + 8) = 2(20) = 40 metres
• Therefore, the answer is B because the perimeter of the classroom is 40 metres

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `7c6cbd18-20b6-487c-a5fb-e4cb3fcc9408`

**Question:**
> A rectangular tablet screen has a length of 24 cm and a width of 18 cm. A software update adds a uniform border around the screen that is 3 cm wide on all sides. What is the area of the border only?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 432 cm²
2. [ ] B) 288 cm²
3. [ ] C) 144 cm²
4. [ ] D) 468 cm²
5. [ ] E) 324 cm²

**Solution:**
> • Original screen dimensions: 24 cm × 18 cm, with area = 24 × 18 = 432 cm²
• With border, new dimensions: length = 24 + 3 + 3 = 30 cm, width = 18 + 3 + 3 = 24 cm
• Total area with border = 30 × 24 = 720 cm²
• Area of border only = 720 - 432 = 288 cm²
• Therefore, the answer is B because the border area is found by subtracting the original screen area from the total area including the border

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c2b2a847-8c92-4a68-90ed-e8aab67da866`

**Question:**
> A rectangular sticker has a width of 4 cm and a length of 9 cm. What is the perimeter of the sticker?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 13 cm
2. [ ] B) 26 cm
3. [ ] C) 36 cm
4. [ ] D) 18 cm
5. [ ] E) 22 cm

**Solution:**
> • The perimeter of a rectangle is calculated using the formula: Perimeter = 2(length + width)
• Substituting the values: Perimeter = 2(9 + 4) = 2(13) = 26 cm
• Therefore, the answer is B because the perimeter of the sticker is 26 cm

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `6eb3b486-81d4-4626-82cf-dc730fa17697`

**Question:**
> A triangular sail on a yacht has a base of 6 metres and a height of 8 metres. What is the area of the sail?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 14 m²
2. [ ] B) 24 m²
3. [ ] C) 48 m²
4. [ ] D) 28 m²
5. [ ] E) 32 m²

**Solution:**
> • The area of a triangle is calculated using the formula: Area = ½ × base × height
• Substituting the values: Area = ½ × 6 × 8
• Area = ½ × 48 = 24 m²
• Therefore, the answer is B because the area of the triangular sail is 24 square metres

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 10 mm
2. [ ] B) 24 mm
3. [ ] C) 18 mm
4. [ ] D) 16 mm
5. [ ] E) 20 mm

**Solution:**
> • A hexagon has 6 sides
• Each side measures 4 mm
• Perimeter = 6 × 4 = 24 mm
• Therefore, the answer is B because the perimeter is found by multiplying the number of sides by the length of each side

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Mathematics - Statistics & Data Interpretation - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `7ae167ff-7b94-4e9e-b6fc-be858b98602f`

**Question:**
> A bar graph shows the number of goals scored by a soccer team in their last 8 matches: 3, 1, 4, 2, 3, 5, 3, 1. The team's coach wants to know the range of goals scored. What is the range?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3
2. [ ] B) 4
3. [ ] C) 5
4. [ ] D) 2
5. [ ] E) 1

**Solution:**
> • The range is calculated as the difference between the highest and lowest values in the data set
• Highest number of goals = 5
• Lowest number of goals = 1
• Range = 5 - 1 = 4
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range of goals scored is 4

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `6d55a7b9-21bb-4309-ad40-eec69586951f`

**Question:**
> A table shows the number of hours of sunshine recorded in a coastal town over 9 consecutive days:

Day 1: 7 hours, Day 2: 9 hours, Day 3: 5 hours, Day 4: 9 hours, Day 5: 11 hours, Day 6: 6 hours, Day 7: 9 hours, Day 8: 8 hours, Day 9: 4 hours

What is the difference between the mode and the median of this data?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 0
2. [ ] B) 1
3. [ ] C) 2
4. [ ] D) 3
5. [ ] E) 4

**Solution:**
> • First, arrange the data in order: 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 9, 9, 11
• The mode is the most frequent value: 9 appears three times, so mode = 9
• The median is the middle value: with 9 numbers, the 5th value is the median = 8
• The difference between mode and median: 9 - 8 = 1
• Therefore, the answer is B because the difference is 1 hour

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `5700a60e-b370-4969-9a04-51983f346eec`

**Question:**
> A histogram shows the number of trees planted by a conservation group over 7 weeks: 16, 23, 19, 16, 28, 21, 16. What is the range of trees planted?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 16
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 19
4. [ ] D) 28
5. [ ] E) 7

**Solution:**
> • To find the range, identify the highest and lowest values in the data set
• Highest value: 28 trees (Week 5)
• Lowest value: 16 trees (Weeks 1, 4, and 7)
• Range = Highest value - Lowest value = 28 - 16 = 12
• Therefore, the answer is B because the range of trees planted is 12

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `44560f92-2bde-47cb-97e4-9cbfc7d3acc4`

**Question:**
> A museum recorded the number of visitors each day over one week:

Monday: 156 visitors
Tuesday: 142 visitors
Wednesday: 168 visitors
Thursday: 142 visitors
Friday: 185 visitors
Saturday: 201 visitors
Sunday: 178 visitors

What is the mean number of visitors per day?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 168
2. [ ] B) 168
3. [ ] C) 142
4. [ ] D) 178
5. [ ] E) 59

**Solution:**
> • To find the mean, add all values: 156 + 142 + 168 + 142 + 185 + 201 + 178 = 1172
• Divide by the number of days: 1172 ÷ 7 = 167.43...
• Round to nearest whole number: 168
• Therefore, the answer is A because the mean number of visitors per day is 168

> A technology store recorded the number of laptops sold each month over 7 months: 34, 28, 41, 28, 35, 28, 45. The store manager wants to know which statistic best represents the most frequently occurring sales figure. What is the mode of this data set?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 28
2. [ ] B) 34
3. [ ] C) 35
4. [ ] D) 41
5. [ ] E) 45

**Solution:**
> • The mode is the value that appears most frequently in a data set
• Count the frequency of each value: 28 appears 3 times, 34 appears 1 time, 35 appears 1 time, 41 appears 1 time, 45 appears 1 time
• The value 28 appears more frequently than any other value
• Therefore, the answer is A because the mode is 28

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Mathematics - Applied Word Problems - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3e47f765-5124-4c5e-98cb-3f802f4df0f3`

**Question:**
> A photography club is printing photos for an exhibition. Each photo costs $1.80 to print, and they need to rent display frames at $3.50 each. If the club has a budget of $150 and needs to print and frame 24 photos, how much money will they have left over?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $21.60
2. [ ] B) $22.80
3. [ ] C) $42.00
4. [ ] D) $127.20
5. [ ] E) $150.00

**Solution:**
> • Cost to print 24 photos = 24 × $1.80 = $43.20
• Cost to rent 24 frames = 24 × $3.50 = $84.00
• Total cost = $43.20 + $84.00 = $127.20
• Money left over = $150.00 - $127.20 = $22.80
• Therefore, the answer is B because after spending $127.20 on printing and framing, they have $22.80 remaining from their $150 budget.

1. [ ] A) 1.86
2. [ ] B) 1.96
3. [ ] C) 18.6
4. [ ] D) 1.76
5. [ ] E) 2.06

**Solution:**
> • Multiply as whole numbers: 248 × 75 = 18,600
• Count decimal places: 2.48 has 2 decimal places, 0.75 has 2 decimal places, total is 4 decimal places
• Place decimal point: 18,600 with 4 decimal places becomes 1.8600 = 1.86
• Therefore, the answer is A because 2.48 × 0.75 = 1.86 centimetres

---

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/diagnostic - Mathematics - Algebra & Equation Solving - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 10
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `d0c4cf5e-f41c-4ebc-bf2f-af0476c0ce22`

**Question:**
> Solve for x: 7x - 3(x + 4) = 2(x - 6)

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 0
2. [ ] B) -6
3. [ ] C) 3
4. [ ] D) 12
5. [ ] E) -12

**Solution:**
> • Expand both sides: 7x - 3x - 12 = 2x - 12
• Simplify left side: 4x - 12 = 2x - 12
• Subtract 2x from both sides: 2x - 12 = -12
• Add 12 to both sides: 2x = 0
• Divide by 2: x = 0
• Therefore, the answer is A because x = 0

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `199c1639-c153-4136-8e9a-f5735c7dc3c7`

**Question:**
> A robotics team programs a robot to navigate a maze. The robot's position after completing several turns is calculated using the equation 5(x - 2) + 3x = 38. What is the value of x?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 6
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 7

**Solution:**
> • Expand the left side: 5(x - 2) + 3x = 5x - 10 + 3x = 8x - 10
• Set up the equation: 8x - 10 = 38
• Add 10 to both sides: 8x = 48
• Divide both sides by 8: x = 6
• Therefore, the answer is B because x = 6

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `05453729-ea5c-4825-8f8a-ccb574bc6ae6`

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 33
2. [ ] B) 51
3. [ ] C) 42
4. [ ] D) 48
5. [ ] E) 39

**Solution:**
> • Substitute g = 6 into the expression: 7g - 9
• Calculate: 7(6) - 9 = 42 - 9 = 33
• Therefore, the answer is A because when g = 6, the expression evaluates to 33

4. [ ] D) 11
5. [ ] E) -7

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_1 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Series & Pattern Recognition - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 13
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `33ca121c-84d8-44cb-b787-fb82f8f470b1`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 1, 3, 7, 15, 31, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 59
2. [ ] B) 63
3. [ ] C) 61
4. [ ] D) 65
5. [ ] E) 67

**Solution:**
> • Each term is obtained by doubling the previous term and adding 1
• 1 × 2 + 1 = 3
• 3 × 2 + 1 = 7
• 7 × 2 + 1 = 15
• 15 × 2 + 1 = 31
• 31 × 2 + 1 = 63
• Therefore, the answer is B because following the pattern of doubling and adding 1 gives us 63

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8
2. [ ] B) 10
3. [ ] C) 12
4. [ ] D) 16
5. [ ] E) 20

**Solution:**
> • Find the differences between consecutive terms: 94-100=-6, 82-94=-12, 64-82=-18, 40-64=-24
• The differences form a pattern: -6, -12, -18, -24 (decreasing by 6 each time)
• The next difference should be -30
• Therefore, the answer is B because 40 + (-30) = 10

**ID:** `77c82549-6a0e-47b5-a0bb-47f3963f33ba`

**Question:**
> A sports coach records the number of laps completed by three swimmers during training. Study the pattern in the grid below. What number should replace the question mark?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 15
2. [ ] B) 18
3. [ ] C) 21
4. [ ] D) 24
5. [ ] E) 27

**Solution:**
> • Each row follows the pattern: first number × 1, first number × 2, first number × 3
• Row 1: 5×1=5, 5×2=10, 5×3=15
• Row 2: 7×1=7, 7×2=14, 7×3=21
• Row 3: 6×1=6, 6×2=12, 6×3=?
• Therefore, the answer is B because 6×3=18

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 48
2. [ ] B) 54
3. [ ] C) 60
4. [ ] D) 64
5. [ ] E) 72

**Solution:**
> • Looking at the pattern across rows and columns: each number in the third column equals the sum of the first two numbers in that row, multiplied by the row number.
• Row 1: (4 + 5) × 1 = 9 × 1 = 9
• Row 2: (6 + 3) × 2 = 9 × 2 = 18
• Row 3: (7 + 11) × 3 = 18 × 3 = 54
• Therefore, the answer is B because 54 is the result of applying the pattern (7 + 11) × 3.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 15
2. [ ] B) 30
3. [ ] C) 60
4. [ ] D) 120
5. [ ] E) 210

**Solution:**
> • Find the prime factorization of 60: 60 = 2 × 2 × 3 × 5
• The distinct prime factors are 2, 3, and 5
• Product of prime factors: 2 × 3 × 5 = 30
• Therefore, the answer is B because the product of all prime factors (2, 3, and 5) equals 30

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 7
3. [ ] C) 9
4. [ ] D) 11
5. [ ] E) 13

**Solution:**
> • √225 = 15 (because 15 × 15 = 225)
• √64 = 8 (because 8 × 8 = 64)
• 15 - 8 = 7
• Therefore, the answer is B because √225 - √64 = 15 - 8 = 7

4. [ ] D) 24
5. [ ] E) 26

**Solution:**

• Count how many numbers there are: 4 numbers
• Divide the sum by the count: 84 ÷ 4 = 21
• Therefore, the answer is B because the average (mean) is 21

• Therefore, the answer is B because following the order of operations (exponents first, then multiplication, then subtraction) gives us 28

> What is the next number in the sequence? 4, 9, 19, 39, 79, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 149
2. [ ] B) 159
3. [ ] C) 169
4. [ ] D) 179
5. [ ] E) 189

**Solution:**
> • Each term is found by multiplying the previous term by 2 and then adding 1
• 4 × 2 + 1 = 9
• 9 × 2 + 1 = 19
• 19 × 2 + 1 = 39
• 39 × 2 + 1 = 79
• 79 × 2 + 1 = 159
• Therefore, the answer is B because the pattern is multiply by 2 and add 1

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `9537f2e5-c855-4312-9a3e-2333b44efdda`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 3, 5, 9, 17, 33, 65, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 97
2. [ ] B) 113
3. [ ] C) 129
4. [ ] D) 131
5. [ ] E) 145

**Solution:**
> • Each term is found by multiplying the previous term by 2 and subtracting 1
• 3 × 2 - 1 = 5, then 5 × 2 - 1 = 9, then 9 × 2 - 1 = 17
• Continuing: 17 × 2 - 1 = 33, then 33 × 2 - 1 = 65, then 65 × 2 - 1 = 129
• Therefore, the answer is C because 129 follows the pattern of doubling and subtracting 1

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 50 points
2. [ ] B) 60 points
3. [ ] C) 70 points
4. [ ] D) 80 points
5. [ ] E) 90 points

**Solution:**
> • First two quarters combined: 18 + 22 = 40 points
• Third quarter score: 40 ÷ 2 = 20 points
• Total after three quarters: 40 + 20 = 60 points
• Therefore, the answer is B because the team scored 60 points in total after three quarters.

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Matrices & Grid Patterns - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 12
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `49077850-41e9-4eed-9efa-8cc6f79f9331`

**Question:**
> A librarian organizes books returned each week. Study the pattern in the grid below. What number should replace the question mark?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 48
2. [ ] B) 54
3. [ ] C) 56
4. [ ] D) 60
5. [ ] E) 63

**Solution:**
> • The pattern works by adding the first two numbers in each row, then multiplying the sum by 3 to get the third number.
• Row 1: (4 + 2) × 3 = 6 × 3 = 18
• Row 2: (5 + 3) × 3 = 8 × 3 = 24
• Row 3: (7 + 11) × 3 = 18 × 3 = 54
• Therefore, the answer is B because 54 is the result of adding 7 and 11, then multiplying by 3.

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `80dae930-deab-470d-a2c2-782a56a26363`

**Question:**

4. [ ] D) 24
5. [ ] E) 26

• Row 1: 3×2=6, 3×4=12, 3×6=18
• Row 2: 4×2=8, 4×4=16, 4×6=24
• Row 3: 5×2=10, 5×4=?, 5×6=30
• Therefore, the answer is B because 5×4=20

**Question:**
> A lighthouse keeper records the number of ships passing by during three different watch periods. Study the pattern in the grid below. What number should replace the question mark?

[Grid: Row 1: 4, 3, 7 | Row 2: 6, 2, 8 | Row 3: 5, 4, ?]

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 7
2. [ ] B) 9
3. [ ] C) 10
4. [ ] D) 11
5. [ ] E) 12

**Solution:**
> • Examine the relationship between the three numbers in each row
• Row 1: 4 + 3 = 7 (the sum of the first two numbers equals the third number)
• Row 2: 6 + 2 = 8 (the pattern holds)
• Row 3: 5 + 4 = 9 (applying the same pattern)
• Therefore, the answer is B because the third number in each row is the sum of the first two numbers, so 5 + 4 = 9

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_2 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Properties & Operations - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `e0987ab7-f963-4ab1-b53a-5769e2f11364`

**Question:**
> What is the value of 6² ÷ 4 + 5?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 11
2. [ ] B) 14
3. [ ] C) 16
4. [ ] D) 18
5. [ ] E) 20

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate 6² = 6 × 6 = 36
• Then divide by 4: 36 ÷ 4 = 9
• Finally, add 5: 9 + 5 = 14
• Therefore, the answer is B because following the order of operations (exponents first, then division, then addition) gives us 14.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 25
3. [ ] C) 75
4. [ ] D) 125
5. [ ] E) 625

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate 5³ = 5 × 5 × 5 = 125
• Then divide by 5: 125 ÷ 5 = 25
• Therefore, the answer is B because 5³ ÷ 5 = 125 ÷ 5 = 25

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 3
2. [ ] B) 4
3. [ ] C) 5
4. [ ] D) 6
5. [ ] E) 7

**Solution:**
> • A prime number is only divisible by 1 and itself
• Check each number between 40 and 60: 41 (prime), 43 (prime), 47 (prime), 53 (prime), 59 (prime)
• Numbers like 42, 44, 45, 46, 48, 49, 50, 51, 52, 54, 55, 56, 57, 58 are composite (have factors other than 1 and themselves)
• Therefore, the answer is C because there are exactly 5 prime numbers in this range

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `515b9f6a-12bc-4694-8403-5c22b214a8eb`

**Question:**
> What is the value of (3³ + √100) ÷ 37 × 37?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 1
2. [ ] B) 37
3. [ ] C) 27
4. [ ] D) 47
5. [ ] E) 370

**Solution:**
> • Calculate 3³ = 3 × 3 × 3 = 27
• Calculate √100 = 10
• Add these values: 27 + 10 = 37
• Divide by 37: 37 ÷ 37 = 1
• Multiply by 37: 1 × 37 = 37
• Therefore, the answer is B because (27 + 10) ÷ 37 × 37 = 37 ÷ 37 × 37 = 1 × 37 = 37

4. [ ] D) 16
5. [ ] E) 18

**Solution:**

• 12 × 12 = 144
• Therefore, the answer is B because √144 = 12

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Series & Pattern Recognition - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 13
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b79e4d2e-7b29-467e-a768-c5c96e34351a`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 1, 3, 7, 15, 31, 63, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 119
2. [ ] B) 127
3. [ ] C) 125
4. [ ] D) 131
5. [ ] E) 135

**Solution:**
> • Each term follows the pattern: 2^n - 1, where n is the position number
• 2^1 - 1 = 1, 2^2 - 1 = 3, 2^3 - 1 = 7, 2^4 - 1 = 15, 2^5 - 1 = 31, 2^6 - 1 = 63
• Alternatively, each term is double the previous term plus 1: (1×2)+1=3, (3×2)+1=7, (7×2)+1=15, (15×2)+1=31, (31×2)+1=63
• Therefore, the answer is B because (63×2)+1 = 127, or 2^7 - 1 = 127

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `11f513df-3472-4f57-89d0-1de9335360bd`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 7, 11, 19, 35, 67, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 127
2. [ ] B) 131
3. [ ] C) 133
4. [ ] D) 135
5. [ ] E) 139

**Solution:**
> • Find the differences between consecutive terms: 11-7=4, 19-11=8, 35-19=16, 67-35=32
• The differences form the pattern: 4, 8, 16, 32 (each difference doubles)
• The next difference should be 32×2=64
• Therefore, the answer is B because 67+64=131

2. [ ] B) 217

• 1³ + 1 = 2, 2³ + 1 = 9, 3³ + 1 = 28, 4³ + 1 = 65, 5³ + 1 = 126
• The next term is 6³ + 1 = 216 + 1 = 217
• Therefore, the answer is B because the pattern is consecutive cubes plus one

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_3 - Numerical Reasoning - Word Problems & Applied Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `83d3956d-99f1-49f3-a0c3-dd21c85442f9`

**Question:**
> A museum charges $7 for adult tickets and $4 for child tickets. On Saturday, the museum sold 35 adult tickets and 48 child tickets. How much money did the museum collect from ticket sales?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $337
2. [ ] B) $437
3. [ ] C) $472
4. [ ] D) $537
5. [ ] E) $583

**Solution:**
> • Adult ticket revenue: 35 × $7 = $245
• Child ticket revenue: 48 × $4 = $192
• Total revenue: $245 + $192 = $437
• Therefore, the answer is B because the museum collected $437 in total from both adult and child ticket sales

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `a09f3d1f-f4e5-495d-a763-d90c05f7731b`

**Question:**
> A school cafeteria serves 240 students lunch each day. Each student receives one carton of milk. If milk cartons come in boxes of 24, how many boxes does the cafeteria need each day?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 8
2. [ ] B) 10
3. [ ] C) 12
4. [ ] D) 15
5. [ ] E) 20

**Solution:**
> • Total students = 240
• Each box contains 24 cartons
• Number of boxes needed = 240 ÷ 24 = 10
• Therefore, the answer is B because the cafeteria needs 10 boxes to provide milk for all 240 students

**ID:** `3fc1bf5b-340f-4a76-be5f-788a7d31f30a`

**Question:**
> A gardener plants tulip bulbs in rows. She plants 7 rows with 12 bulbs in each row. If each bulb costs $2, how much did she spend on tulip bulbs in total?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $84
2. [ ] B) $168
3. [ ] C) $140
4. [ ] D) $96
5. [ ] E) $154

**Solution:**
> • First, find the total number of bulbs: 7 rows × 12 bulbs = 84 bulbs
• Then, calculate the total cost: 84 bulbs × $2 = $168
• Therefore, the answer is B because the gardener spent $168 on tulip bulbs in total.

**ID:** `ae2c4f50-0e77-42c1-a9cf-7d6d39b041c6`

**Question:**
> A farmer collects eggs from his chickens over three days. On Monday he collects 84 eggs, on Tuesday he collects 96 eggs, and on Wednesday he collects 72 eggs. He packs the eggs into cartons that hold 12 eggs each. How many cartons does he fill?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 18
2. [ ] B) 21
3. [ ] C) 24
4. [ ] D) 252
5. [ ] E) 28

**Solution:**
> • Total eggs collected = 84 + 96 + 72 = 252 eggs
• Number of cartons = 252 ÷ 12 = 21 cartons
• Therefore, the answer is B because the farmer fills 21 cartons with all the eggs collected over the three days.

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $495
2. [ ] B) $585
3. [ ] C) $630
4. [ ] D) $675
5. [ ] E) $810

**Solution:**
> • First, find how many members still need to pay: 18 - 5 = 13 members
• Each member needs to pay $45, so multiply: 13 × $45 = $585
• Therefore, the answer is B because $585 still needs to be collected from the 13 members who haven't paid yet

**ID:** `f306671a-a9a5-4252-a215-aff3b9e1e200`

**Question:**
> A florist arranges roses in bouquets for three different events. Study the pattern in the grid below. What number should replace the question mark?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 24
2. [ ] B) 27
3. [ ] C) 30
4. [ ] D) 33
5. [ ] E) 36

**Solution:**
> • Each row follows the pattern where the first number is multiplied by 1, 2, and 3
• Row 1: 8×1=8, 8×2=16, 8×3=24
• Row 2: 9×1=9, 9×2=18, 9×3=27
• Row 3: 10×1=10, 10×2=20, so 10×3=30 should be in the third position
• The missing value is in Row 2, Column 3: 9×3=27
• Therefore, the answer is B because 27 completes the multiplication pattern for Row 2

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3e5d49c3-113a-4021-ac20-2a8c147693c2`

**Question:**
> What is the smallest positive integer that has exactly 6 factors?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 18
4. [ ] D) 20
5. [ ] E) 24

**Solution:**
> • To find factors systematically, we test small positive integers:
• 6 has factors: 1, 2, 3, 6 (4 factors)
• 8 has factors: 1, 2, 4, 8 (4 factors)
• 10 has factors: 1, 2, 5, 10 (4 factors)
• 12 has factors: 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 12 (6 factors)
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 is the smallest positive integer with exactly 6 factors

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 54
2. [ ] B) 54
3. [ ] C) 72
4. [ ] D) 78
5. [ ] E) 234

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate 9² = 81
• Then, calculate √81 = 9
• Next, multiply 9 × 3 = 27
• Finally, subtract: 81 - 27 = 54
• Therefore, the answer is B because following the order of operations (exponents and roots first, then multiplication, then subtraction) gives us 54

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_4 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Series & Pattern Recognition - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 13
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `824c9da1-b0c0-4858-9f2b-e60532254a2e`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 4, 10, 22, 46, 94, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 186
2. [ ] B) 190
3. [ ] C) 188
4. [ ] D) 192
5. [ ] E) 194

**Solution:**
> • Each term is found by multiplying the previous term by 2 and then adding 2
• 4 × 2 + 2 = 10, then 10 × 2 + 2 = 22, then 22 × 2 + 2 = 46, then 46 × 2 + 2 = 94
• Therefore, the answer is B because 94 × 2 + 2 = 190

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `8b53daef-a02c-4bc6-ae0d-40fde345dc62`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 1, 2, 4, 7, 13, 24, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 40
2. [ ] B) 44
3. [ ] C) 48
4. [ ] D) 52
5. [ ] E) 56

**Solution:**
> • Each term is the sum of all previous terms: 1, 1+1=2, 1+1+2=4, 1+1+2+4=8 (wait, checking pattern differently)
• Actually: 1, 2 (1+1), 4 (1+2+1), 7 (2+4+1), 13 (4+7+2), 24 (7+13+4)
• Pattern: each term = sum of previous two terms plus the term before that, minus a correction. Let me verify: 1→2 (+1), 2→4 (+2), 4→7 (+3), 7→13 (+6), 13→24 (+11)
• Differences: 1, 2, 3, 6, 11... Next difference pattern: 1, 2, 3 (1+2), 6 (2+3+1), 11 (3+6+2)
• Each difference is the sum of the previous two differences: 1+2=3, 2+3=5 (no), trying again: differences are 1, 2, 3, 6, 11
• The pattern in differences: 1, 2, 3, 6 (2+3+1), 11 (3+6+2), next is 6+11+3=20
• Actually simpler: each term equals sum of previous two terms plus term three positions back: 7+13+4=24, so 13+24+7=44
• Therefore, the answer is B because 24+20=44

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `a8fc2770-4eff-4dfb-9735-e3cbbdc3951d`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 2, 3, 5, 7, 11, 13, 17, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 18
2. [ ] B) 19
3. [ ] C) 20
4. [ ] D) 21
5. [ ] E) 22

**Solution:**
> • This sequence consists of prime numbers in ascending order: 2, 3, 5, 7, 11, 13, 17
• A prime number is a number greater than 1 that has no positive divisors other than 1 and itself
• After 17, we need to find the next prime number
• 18 = 2 × 9 (not prime), 19 has no divisors other than 1 and 19 (prime)
• Therefore, the answer is B because 19 is the next prime number after 17

> What is the next number in the sequence? 10, 13, 19, 28, 40, 55, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 68
2. [ ] B) 70
3. [ ] C) 73
4. [ ] D) 75
5. [ ] E) 78

**Solution:**
> • The differences between consecutive terms are: 13-10=3, 19-13=6, 28-19=9, 40-28=12, 55-40=15
• The differences form the pattern: 3, 6, 9, 12, 15 (multiples of 3, increasing by 3 each time)
• The next difference should be 18

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `a268ac20-24d1-4256-ada9-85c0b6a34725`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 128, 64, 32, 16, 8, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 2
2. [ ] B) 4
3. [ ] C) 6
4. [ ] D) 5
5. [ ] E) 3

**Solution:**
> • Each number is divided by 2 to get the next number
• 128 ÷ 2 = 64, 64 ÷ 2 = 32, 32 ÷ 2 = 16, 16 ÷ 2 = 8
• 8 ÷ 2 = 4
• Therefore, the answer is B because the pattern continues by halving each term

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b2b5a77f-a09b-47ac-8a80-77bbc1a180ee`

**Question:**
> A school is organizing a science fair. Each display table costs $12 to rent and each participant receives a certificate that costs $3 to print. If there are 15 display tables and 42 participants, what is the total cost?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $126
2. [ ] B) $306
3. [ ] C) $180
4. [ ] D) $252
5. [ ] E) $234

**Solution:**
> • Cost of renting tables: 15 × $12 = $180
• Cost of certificates: 42 × $3 = $126
• Total cost: $180 + $126 = $306
• Therefore, the answer is B because the total cost for both tables and certificates is $306

• Number of rows = 8

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) $5
2. [ ] B) $6
3. [ ] C) $7
4. [ ] D) $8
5. [ ] E) $10

**Solution:**
> • First day late fee: $2
• Additional days overdue: 5 - 1 = 4 days
• Additional days fee: 4 × $1 = $4
• Total late fee: $2 + $4 = $6

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 21
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 27
4. [ ] D) 30
5. [ ] E) 33

• Row 1: 3×1=3, 3×2=6, 3×3=9

5. [ ] E) 56

**Solution:**

• Row 1: (4 × 6) ÷ 2 = 24 ÷ 2 = 12
• Row 2: (8 × 5) ÷ 2 = 40 ÷ 2 = 20
• Row 3: (12 × 8) ÷ 2 = 96 ÷ 2 = 48
• Therefore, the answer is B because 48 is the result of applying the pattern (12 × 8) ÷ 2.

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `57e31c4e-a63b-4834-b50f-68d6273d3d73`

**Question:**
> What is the value of 6² - √81?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 24
2. [ ] B) 27
3. [ ] C) 30
4. [ ] D) 33
5. [ ] E) 36

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate 6² = 6 × 6 = 36
• Next, calculate √81 = 9 (because 9 × 9 = 81)
• Then subtract: 36 - 9 = 27
• Therefore, the answer is B because 6² - √81 = 36 - 9 = 27

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `f0dd70d6-1322-4575-a922-a19ff050bec4`

**Question:**
> What is the average of the first four even numbers?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 5
3. [ ] C) 6
4. [ ] D) 8
5. [ ] E) 10

**Solution:**
> • The first four even numbers are 2, 4, 6, and 8
• To find the average, add them together: 2 + 4 + 6 + 8 = 20
• Divide by the count of numbers: 20 ÷ 4 = 5
• Therefore, the answer is B because the average of 2, 4, 6, and 8 is 5

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `43ecc2bb-1179-4d86-a7ad-6a7280ef8b61`

**Question:**
> If the product of two consecutive even numbers is 168, what is their sum?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 24
2. [ ] B) 26
3. [ ] C) 28
4. [ ] D) 30
5. [ ] E) 32

**Solution:**
> • Let the two consecutive even numbers be n and n+2
• Their product is n(n+2) = 168
• Testing even numbers: 12 × 14 = 168 ✓
• The sum is 12 + 14 = 26
• Therefore, the answer is B because the two consecutive even numbers that multiply to 168 are 12 and 14, and their sum is 26

---

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 4
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 36
4. [ ] D) 48
5. [ ] E) 96

**Solution:**
> • Multiples of 8: 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48...
• Multiples of 12: 12, 24, 36, 48, 60...
• The lowest common multiple is the smallest number that appears in both lists: 24
• Therefore, the answer is B because 24 is the smallest number divisible by both 8 and 12.

3. [ ] C) 21
4. [ ] D) 23
5. [ ] E) 25

**Solution:**
> • √121 = 11 (because 11 × 11 = 121)
• 2³ = 2 × 2 × 2 = 8
• 11 + 8 = 19
• Therefore, the answer is B because √121 + 2³ = 11 + 8 = 19

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Series & Pattern Recognition - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 13
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `10c207f3-26b6-49a2-af4d-350aaa99f13c`

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 100, 95, 85, 70, 50, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 20
2. [ ] B) 25
3. [ ] C) 30
4. [ ] D) 35
5. [ ] E) 40

**Solution:**
> • The differences between consecutive terms are: 95-100=-5, 85-95=-10, 70-85=-15, 50-70=-20
• The differences form a pattern: -5, -10, -15, -20 (decreasing by 5 each time)
• The next difference should be -25
• Therefore, the answer is B because 50 - 25 = 25

1. [ ] A) 55
2. [ ] B) 50

4. [ ] D) 40
5. [ ] E) 52

• Following this pattern: 60 - 10 = 50
• Therefore, the answer is B because the next number in the sequence is 50

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 3, 8, 18, 38, 78, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 148
2. [ ] B) 158
3. [ ] C) 168
4. [ ] D) 178
5. [ ] E) 188

**Solution:**
> • Each term is found by multiplying the previous term by 2 and then adding 2
• 3 × 2 + 2 = 8
• 8 × 2 + 2 = 18
• 18 × 2 + 2 = 38
• 38 × 2 + 2 = 78
• 78 × 2 + 2 = 158
• Therefore, the answer is B because following the pattern of doubling and adding 2, the next number is 158

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**Question:**
> What is the next number in the sequence? 4, 6, 10, 18, 34, ?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 62
2. [ ] B) 66
3. [ ] C) 68
4. [ ] D) 70
5. [ ] E) 72

**Solution:**
> • Each term is found by doubling the previous term and subtracting 2
• 4 × 2 - 2 = 6, then 6 × 2 - 2 = 10, then 10 × 2 - 2 = 18, then 18 × 2 - 2 = 34
• Following this pattern: 34 × 2 - 2 = 68 - 2 = 66
• Therefore, the answer is B because 66 is the next term in the sequence

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Numerical Reasoning - Word Problems & Applied Reasoning - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 13
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `2c4d288e-454b-4ad6-9a12-5523b2bd7628`

**Question:**
> A wildlife photographer takes photos on a safari trip. She takes 156 photos over 6 days, taking the same number of photos each day. If her camera's memory card can store 320 photos in total, how many more photos can she take before the card is full?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 138
2. [ ] B) 164
3. [ ] C) 182
4. [ ] D) 196
5. [ ] E) 214

**Solution:**
> • First, find how many photos she takes per day: 156 ÷ 6 = 26 photos per day (not needed for final answer, but confirms equal distribution)
• Photos already taken: 156
• Memory card capacity: 320 photos
• Photos remaining: 320 - 156 = 164 photos
• Therefore, the answer is B because she can take 164 more photos before the card is full.

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `1b73b89b-263f-4eda-9c8e-717574c95b9e`

**Question:**
> A school band is selling chocolate bars to raise money for new instruments. Each chocolate bar costs $4. The band needs to raise $360. If they have already sold 67 chocolate bars, how many more do they need to sell to reach their goal?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 23
2. [ ] B) 24
3. [ ] C) 25
4. [ ] D) 90
5. [ ] E) 157

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate how much money has been raised: 67 × $4 = $268
• Next, find how much more money is needed: $360 - $268 = $92
• Finally, divide by the price per bar: $92 ÷ $4 = 23
• Therefore, the answer is A because the band needs to sell 23 more chocolate bars to reach their goal of $360.

|  8  |  3  | 11 |
|  5  |  9  | 14 |
| 12  |  ?  | 19 |

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 5
2. [ ] B) 7
3. [ ] C) 8
4. [ ] D) 9
5. [ ] E) 10

**Solution:**
> • In each row, the third number equals the sum of the first two numbers
• Row 1: 8 + 3 = 11 ✓

• Row 3: 12 + ? = 19
• Therefore, ? = 19 - 12 = 7
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 + 7 = 19

### EduTest Scholarship (Year 7 Entry)/practice_5 - Numerical Reasoning - Number Properties & Operations - multiple_choice

**Total Questions in DB:** 12
**Sampled Questions:** 5

#### Question 1 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `27b40e0d-35ba-4346-9cf2-b2c24d003e7c`

**Question:**
> A number is multiplied by 3, then 15 is added to the result, and finally this sum is divided by 4 to give 12. What is the original number?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 9
2. [ ] B) 11
3. [ ] C) 13
4. [ ] D) 15
5. [ ] E) 17

**Solution:**
> • Working backwards from the final result of 12:
• Before dividing by 4, the sum was 12 × 4 = 48
• Before adding 15, the result was 48 - 15 = 33
• Before multiplying by 3, the original number was 33 ÷ 3 = 11
• Check: (11 × 3 + 15) ÷ 4 = (33 + 15) ÷ 4 = 48 ÷ 4 = 12 ✓
• Therefore, the answer is B because the original number is 11

---

#### Question 2 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `c482406d-da47-4ee9-974a-6fcc6f6b284d`

**Question:**
> What is the least common multiple (LCM) of 12 and 18?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 6
2. [ ] B) 36
3. [ ] C) 54
4. [ ] D) 72
5. [ ] E) 216

**Solution:**
> • Find the prime factorization: 12 = 2² × 3 and 18 = 2 × 3²
• Take the highest power of each prime factor: 2² and 3²
• LCM = 2² × 3² = 4 × 9 = 36
• Therefore, the answer is B because 36 is the smallest number that both 12 and 18 divide into evenly.

---

#### Question 3 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `b53c82d0-1382-4af3-aeb0-0db1c0a0f055`

**Question:**
> What is the value of 2³ × 5 + √49?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 45
2. [ ] B) 47
3. [ ] C) 49
4. [ ] D) 51
5. [ ] E) 53

**Solution:**
> • First, calculate 2³ = 2 × 2 × 2 = 8
• Then, multiply by 5: 8 × 5 = 40
• Calculate √49 = 7 (because 7 × 7 = 49)
• Add the results: 40 + 7 = 47
• Therefore, the answer is B because 2³ × 5 + √49 = 8 × 5 + 7 = 40 + 7 = 47

---

#### Question 4 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `3ea305dc-9a17-405e-9a7c-2e37aa3115ec`

**Question:**
> A number is multiplied by 4, then 15 is added to the result, giving 63. What is the original number?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 10
2. [ ] B) 12
3. [ ] C) 14
4. [ ] D) 16
5. [ ] E) 18

**Solution:**
> • Working backwards: if the final result is 63, then before adding 15, the value was 63 - 15 = 48
• This value of 48 was obtained by multiplying the original number by 4
• Therefore, the original number is 48 ÷ 4 = 12
• Therefore, the answer is B because 12 × 4 + 15 = 48 + 15 = 63

---

#### Question 5 ✅ (PASS)

**ID:** `ce46b197-869e-439c-aaa9-0d36ae22da0a`

**Question:**
> What is the value of √144 + 3²?

**Options:**
1. [ ] A) 15
2. [ ] B) 21
3. [ ] C) 19
4. [ ] D) 18
5. [ ] E) 24

**Solution:**
> • First, find the square root of 144: √144 = 12 (since 12 × 12 = 144)
• Next, calculate 3² = 3 × 3 = 9
• Add the two results: 12 + 9 = 21
• Therefore, the answer is B because √144 + 3² = 12 + 9 = 21
